[{'tool_use_id': 'toolu_bdrk_01DENiG4xBYCVWuM1StiHUq8', 'type': 'tool_result', 'content': [{'type': 'text', 'text': 'I now have a thorough understanding of the entire neuron architecture as it relates to chunked prefill. Here is my comprehensive report.\n\n---\n\n## Comprehensive Report: Neuron-Specific Constraints for Chunked Prefill Implementation\n\n### 1. KV Cache Management on Neuron\n\n**Key files:**\n- `/opt/aws_neuronx_venv_pytorch_inference_vllm_0_16/lib/python3.12/site-packages/vllm_neuron/worker/neuron_worker.py`\n- `/opt/aws_neuronx_venv_pytorch_inference_vllm_0_16/lib/python3.12/site-packages/neuronx_distributed_inference/modules/kvcache/block_kv_cache_manager.py`\n- `/opt/aws_neuronx_venv_pytorch_inference_vllm_0_16/lib/python3.12/site-packages/neuronx_distributed_inference/modules/kvcache/kv_cache_manager.py`\n\n**Two KV cache layouts exist:**\n\nA. **Contiguous KV layout** (default, non-chunked):\n- Shape: `(batch_size, num_kv_head_per_rank, max_len, head_dim)`\n- Each sequence gets a fixed slot identified by a `seq_id` (called `input_block_ids`)\n- The number of blocks equals `max_num_seqs + 1` (the +1 is a null block)\n- Block size equals `max_model_len` -- meaning each "block" is the entire sequence length\n- Requires sequence-id-based reordering to maintain correct KV cache placement (the `_reordered()` context manager in `NeuronModelBase`)\n\nB. **Block KV layout** (required for chunked prefill and prefix caching):\n- Shape: `(num_blocks, num_kv_heads_per_rank, block_size, head_dim)`\n- Activated when `is_block_kv_layout = True` (set automatically when `enable_chunked_prefill` or `enable_prefix_caching` is true)\n- Uses `slot_mapping` and `block_tables` to manage paged-attention-style cache\n- `BlockKVCacheManager._update_cache_with_index_put()` writes KV using block_id and block_offset derived from slot_mapping\n- The NxDI library manages KV allocation internally under the hood\n\n**Memory determination** (in `NeuronWorker.determine_available_memory()`):\n- For block KV layout: queries Neuron runtime via `torch.classes.neuron.Runtime().get_vnc_memory_stats()`\n- For contiguous layout: manually calculates exact memory as `num_blocks * num_layers * page_size_per_layer`\n\n---\n\n### 2. Model Compilation / Tracing Constraints\n\n**Key files:**\n- `/opt/aws_neuronx_venv_pytorch_inference_vllm_0_16/lib/python3.12/site-packages/neuronx_distributed_inference/models/model_base.py` (lines 3107-3153)\n- `/opt/aws_neuronx_venv_pytorch_inference_vllm_0_16/lib/python3.12/site-packages/neuronx_distributed_inference/models/model_wrapper.py` (lines 180-270)\n- `/opt/aws_neuronx_venv_pytorch_inference_vllm_0_16/lib/python3.12/site-packages/neuronx_distributed_inference/modules/autobucketing.py`\n\n**Critical constraint: Models are compiled with fixed shapes and then traced via `parallel_model_trace()`.**\n\nThe NxDI framework compiles **two separate models**:\n1. **Context Encoding Model (CTE)**: For prefill. Compiled with:\n   - `batch_size = ctx_batch_size` (defaults to 1 for chunked prefill)\n   - `n_active_tokens = max_context_length`\n   - `bucket_n_active_tokens = True` (enables bucketing on the active token dimension)\n   \n2. **Token Generation Model (TKG)**: For decode. Compiled with:\n   - `batch_size = tkg_batch_size` (= max_num_seqs for continuous batching)\n   - `n_active_tokens = 1`\n   - `bucket_n_active_tokens = False`\n\n**Bucketing (compile-time shape flexibility):**\n- Models are compiled for multiple "bucket" shapes to avoid recompilation\n- Context encoding buckets: powers of 2 up to max_context_length (e.g., [128, 256, 512, 1024, ...])\n- For chunked prefill, CTE has 2D bucketing: `[chunk_size, num_tiles]`\n- Inputs are padded to the nearest bucket size at runtime\n- Generated by `generate_buckets_for_cte()` and `generate_buckets_for_tkg()`\n\n**Static shape requirement:**\n- `input_ids` shape: `(batch_size, n_active_tokens)` -- must match compiled shapes\n- `position_ids`: Same shape as input_ids\n- All model inputs are padded to bucket boundaries before execution\n- The model wrapper\'s `input_generator()` produces fixed-shape example inputs for each bucket during compilation\n\n---\n\n### 3. Neuron Platform Configuration\n\n**Key file:** `/opt/aws_neuronx_venv_pytorch_inference_vllm_0_16/lib/python3.12/site-packages/vllm_neuron/platform.py`\n\n**Platform characteristics:**\n- `_enum = PlatformEnum.OOT` (Out-Of-Tree plugin)\n- `device_name = "cpu"` / `device_type = "cpu"` (Neuron uses CPU device type for PyTorch)\n- `supports_v1() = True` (uses vLLM V1 architecture)\n- `is_async_output_supported() = False`\n- `is_pin_memory_available() = False`\n- Worker class: `vllm_neuron.worker.neuron_worker.NeuronWorker`\n- Attention backend: `vllm_neuron.attention.neuron_attn.NeuronAttentionBackend`\n- Supported quantization: `["neuron_quant", "fbgemm_fp8"]`\n\n**What is disabled/overridden:**\n- `ModelConfig.verify_with_parallel_config` -- skipped (attention head divisibility check)\n- `ModelConfig._verify_quantization` -- skipped\n- `ModelConfig._verify_cuda_graph` -- skipped\n- `ModelConfig.get_and_verify_max_len` -- modified to ignore HF sliding_window\n- `world_size_across_dp` -- overridden to return `data_parallel_size` on Neuron\n- Distributed backend: `"gloo"` (not NCCL)\n- `compile_or_warm_up_model()` is a no-op\n\n---\n\n### 4. Chunked Prefill: Current State\n\n**The custom Neuron scheduler DISABLES chunked prefill by default:**\n\nIn `platform.py` line 397:\n```python\nvllm_config.scheduler_config.enable_chunked_prefill = False\n```\n\nThe custom scheduler `ContinuousBatchingNeuronScheduler` is set as the default scheduler class. It:\n- Separates prefill and decode into different scheduling steps (prefill takes priority)\n- Uses a holdback queue to manage which requests are visible to the base scheduler\n- Limits `max_prompt_batch_size = 1` (only one prefill at a time)\n\n**However, chunked prefill CAN be enabled** via `DISABLE_NEURON_CUSTOM_SCHEDULER=1`, which bypasses the custom scheduler and uses vLLM\'s native V1 scheduler with chunked prefill.\n\n**When chunked prefill is enabled:**\n- `is_block_kv_layout` must be True (paged KV cache required)\n- `batch_size = 1` for the CTE model (all requests concatenated into one long sequence along the seq dim)\n- `max_context_length` becomes the chunk size (scheduler\'s `max_num_batched_tokens`)\n- Block size must be explicitly set\n- `ChunkedPrefillConfig` is used with `max_num_seqs`, `kernel_q_tile_size` (default 128), `kernel_kv_tile_size` (default 1024)\n\n**CRITICAL BLOCKER in NxDI:**\n\nIn `/opt/aws_neuronx_venv_pytorch_inference_vllm_0_16/lib/python3.12/site-packages/neuronx_distributed_inference/models/model_base.py` line 3054-3055:\n```python\nif self.neuron_config.is_chunked_prefill:\n    raise NotImplementedError("Chunked Prefill is not available in NxDI for now")\n```\n\nThis means the underlying NxDI library currently raises `NotImplementedError` for chunked prefill, even though the vllm_neuron plugin has full code paths for it.\n\n---\n\n### 5. Continuous Batching on Neuron: Slots and Buckets\n\n**Slot/seq_id system (contiguous KV):**\n- Each request is assigned a `neuron_seq_id` from a pool of `free_seq_ids` (size = `max_num_reqs`)\n- This maps to a specific "line" in the KV cache\n- When a request finishes, its slot is freed back to the pool\n- The model requires inputs sorted by seq_id for correct KV cache access (the `_reordered()` mechanism)\n\n**Block table system (block KV):**\n- Standard vLLM-style paged attention with `block_tables` and `slot_mapping`\n- `slot = block_number * block_size + offset`\n- Padding uses -1 for slot_mapping, 0 for block_table entries\n\n**The `prefill_completion_state` tensor:**\n- A boolean tensor indicating whether each request\'s prefill is complete\n- Used in chunked prefill mode to mask logits of incomplete prefills (set to -inf or -1)\n- Only requests with completed prefills get sampled\n\n---\n\n### 6. Neuron Limitations Regarding Dynamic Shapes, Padding, and Attention\n\n**Static compilation constraints:**\n- All tensor dimensions must match pre-compiled bucket shapes\n- Inputs are padded to the nearest bucket using `make_tensor_with_pad()`\n- For prefill: input tokens padded to `max_seq_len` in the batch\n- For decode: input tokens padded to 1 (single token)\n- Position IDs padded with 0s\n- Block tables padded to `max_blocks_per_seq`\n\n**Attention mechanism constraints:**\n- NeuronAttentionBackend is a stub -- `get_kv_cache_shape()` raises `NotImplementedError`\n- Actual attention is handled entirely within the NxDI compiled model\n- Flash decoding is incompatible with chunked prefill and block KV layout\n- Attention TKG NKI kernels are incompatible with chunked prefill\n- Transposed K cache is incompatible with block KV layout and chunked prefill\n- Batch bucketing (`token_generation_batches`) is incompatible with chunked prefill, prefix caching, and block KV layout\n\n**Chunked prefill attention in NxDI uses a tile grid:**\n- Q tile size: configurable (default 128)\n- KV tile size: configurable (default 1024)\n- Max tiles = `ceil(max_q_len / q_tile_size) * ceil(max_kv_cache_len / kv_tile_size)`\n- 2D bucketing: `[chunk_size, num_tiles]` for CTE model compilation\n\n**`CHUNKED_ATTENTION_SUPPORTED_NEURON_CONFIG` (from NxDI config.py line 24-31) defines what MUST be disabled for chunked attention:**\n```python\n{\n    "flash_decoding_enabled": False,\n    "attn_tkg_builtin_kernel_enabled": False,\n    "attn_tkg_nki_kernel_enabled": False,\n    "is_prefix_caching": False,\n    "is_chunked_prefill": False,\n    "padding_side": "right",\n    "attention_dp_degree": 1,\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### Summary of Key Architectural Constraints for Chunked Prefill Implementation\n\n1. **NxDI currently blocks chunked prefill** with `raise NotImplementedError` -- the vllm_neuron plugin has all the code paths ready, but the underlying NxDI model base does not support it yet.\n\n2. **Block KV layout is mandatory** for chunked prefill. The contiguous layout cannot support it.\n\n3. **CTE model compiled with batch_size=1**: All requests in a chunk are concatenated along the sequence dimension into a single "mega-sequence." This differs fundamentally from GPU chunked prefill where multiple requests retain their own batch dimension.\n\n4. **Static shape compilation**: Every dimension must be padded to pre-compiled bucket sizes. Dynamic shapes are not possible.\n\n5. **Tile-based attention kernel**: Chunked prefill uses a specialized tiled attention approach with configurable Q and KV tile sizes, creating 2D bucket combinations.\n\n6. **Separate prefill/decode models**: The model is compiled as two distinct NEFFs (Neuron Executable File Format). Chunked prefill modifies the CTE model\'s compilation shape but the overall two-model architecture remains.\n\n7. **No async output support**: `is_async_output_supported() = False` limits pipelining options.\n\n8. **Max prompt length enforcement**: Neuron models have a hard `max_context_length` that cannot be exceeded (unlike GPU where it is a soft limit).\n\n9. **Scheduler override mechanism exists**: `DISABLE_NEURON_CUSTOM_SCHEDULER=1` enables vLLM native scheduler with chunked prefill, but will hit the NxDI `NotImplementedError`.\n\n10. **The vllm_neuron model runner already implements full chunked prefill input preparation** (`_prepare_chunked_prefill_inputs`, `_process_new_request_for_chunked_prefill`, `_finalize_chunked_prefill_inputs`) including proper slot mapping, block tables, and `prefill_completion_state` tracking. The implementation is ready pending NxDI support.'}]}]

None if no constraints.\n206\t        Returns:\n207\t            ModelRunnerOutput with sampled tokens\n208\t        """\n209\t        sample_start = time.perf_counter()\n210\t\n211\t        if self._cached_logits is None:\n212\t            raise RuntimeError(\n213\t                "sample_tokens() called without prior execute_model(). Logits must be cached first."\n214\t            )\n215\t\n216\t        hidden_states = self._cached_logits\n217\t        model_input = self._cached_model_input\n218\t\n219\t        # Clear cache\n220\t        self._cached_logits = None\n221\t        self._cached_model_input = None\n222\t\n223\t        # Handle both tensor and list cases (multimodal models may return lists)\n224\t        if isinstance(hidden_states, torch.Tensor):\n225\t            batch_size = hidden_states.shape[0] if hidden_states.dim() > 0 else 0\n226\t        else:\n227\t            batch_size = len(hidden_states) if hidden_states else 0\n228\t\n229\t        # Check if using on-device sampling\n230\t        if self.model.neuron_config.on_device_sampling_config is not None:\n231\t            # On-device (hardware) sampling path\n232\t            # Note: Structured outputs not supported with on-device sampling\n233\t            if (\n234\t                grammar_output is not None\n235\t                and grammar_output.grammar_bitmask is not None\n236\t            ):\n237\t                logger.warning(\n238\t                    "Grammar bitmask provided but on-device sampling is enabled. "\n239\t                    "Structured outputs are not supported with on-device sampling. "\n240\t                    "The grammar bitmask will be ignored."\n241\t                )\n242\t\n243\t            sampling_start = time.perf_counter()\n244\t            sampler_output = self._sample_on_device(hidden_states, model_input)\n245\t            sampling_elapsed = (time.perf_counter() - sampling_start) * 1000\n246\t            logger.debug("[PERF] on_device_sampling: %.2fms", sampling_elapsed)\n247\t        else:\n248\t            # CPU sampling path - supports structured outputs\n249\t            # Prepare logits (handle prefill completion state and reorder)\n250\t            logits = self._prepare_logits_for_sampling(hidden_states, model_input)\n251\t\n252\t            # Apply grammar bitmask if present\n253\t            if (\n254\t                grammar_output is not None\n255\t                and grammar_output.grammar_bitmask is not None\n256\t            ):\n257\t                bitmask_start = time.perf_counter()\n258\t                logits = self._apply_grammar_bitmask_from_output(logits, grammar_output)\n259\t                bitmask_elapsed = (time.perf_counter() - bitmask_start) * 1000\n260\t                logger.debug("[PERF] apply_grammar_bitmask: %.2fms", bitmask_elapsed)\n261\t\n262\t            # Sample from logits\n263\t            sampling_start = time.perf_counter()\n264\t            sampling_metadata = self.input_batch.sampling_metadata\n265\t            if sampling_metadata is None:\n266\t                raise RuntimeError("Sampling metadata not available")\n267\t\n268\t            sampler_output = self.cpu_sampler(logits, sampling_metadata)\n269\t            sampling_elapsed = (time.perf_counter() - sampling_start) * 1000\n270\t            logger.debug("[PERF] cpu_sampling: %.2fms", sampling_elapsed)\n271\t\n272\t        # Generate model runner output\n273\t        output_gen_start = time.perf_counter()\n274\t        result = self._generate_model_runner_output(sampler_output)\n275\t        output_gen_elapsed = (time.perf_counter() - output_gen_start) * 1000\n276\t        logger.debug("[PERF] _generate_model_runner_output: %.2fms", output_gen_elapsed)\n277\t\n278\t        total_elapsed = (time.perf_counter() - sample_start) * 1000\n279\t        logger.debug(\n280\t            "[PERF] sample_tokens total: %.2fms [batch=%d]", total_elapsed, batch_size\n281\t        )\n282\t\n283\t        return result\n284\t\n285\t    def _sample_on_device(\n286\t        self,\n287\t        hidden_states: torch.Tensor,\n288\t        model_input: ModelInputForNeuron,\n289\t    ) -> SamplerOutput:\n290\t        """\n291\t        Perform on-device (hardware) sampling.\n292\t\n293\t        Args:\n294\t            hidden_states: Model output tensor\n295\t            model_input: Model input containing request information\n296\t\n297\t        Returns:\n298\t            SamplerOutput with sampled token IDs\n299\t        """\n300\t        logger.debug("output from model forward: hidden_states=%s", hidden_states)\n301\t\n302\t        # Mask incomplete prefills with -1 (invalid token ID)\n303\t        if model_input.prefill_completion_state is not None:\n304\t            for i, state in enumerate(model_input.prefill_completion_state):\n305\t                if not state.item():\n306\t                    hidden_states[i] = -1\n307\t\n308\t        logger.debug(\n309\t            "output after excluding partial prefill results: hidden_states=%s",\n310\t            hidden_states,\n311\t        )\n312\t\n313\t        # Reorder outputs to match input batch order\n314\t        request_id_order = {\n315\t            request_id: idx for idx, request_id in enumerate(model_input.request_ids)\n316\t        }\n317\t\n318\t        reorder_indices = torch.tensor(\n319\t            [request_id_order[request_id] for request_id in self.input_batch.req_ids]\n320\t        )\n321\t\n322\t        hidden_states = hidden_states[reorder_indices]\n323\t\n324\t        # Perform hardware sampling\n325\t        try:\n326\t            logger.debug(\n327\t                "Using hardware sampling: on_device_sampling_config is configured"\n328\t            )\n329\t            result = self.model.sample(logits=hidden_states)\n330\t            return result\n331\t\n332\t        except Exception as e:\n333\t            logger.error(\n334\t                "Hardware sampling failed for requests %s: %s",\n335\t                model_input.request_ids,\n336\t                str(e),\n337\t            )\n338\t            raise RuntimeError("Hardware sampling operation failed: %s" % str(e)) from e\n339\t\n340\t    def _apply_grammar_bitmask_from_output(\n341\t        self,\n342\t        logits: torch.Tensor,\n343\t        grammar_output: "GrammarOutput",\n344\t    ) -> torch.Tensor:\n345\t        """\n346\t        Apply grammar bitmask from GrammarOutput to logits.\n347\t        Args:\n348\t            logits: [batch_size, vocab_size]\n349\t            grammar_output: Contains grammar_bitmask and structured_output_request_ids\n350\t        Returns:\n351\t            Masked logits (new tensor, not in-place modification)\n352\t        """\n353\t        grammar_bitmask = grammar_output.grammar_bitmask\n354\t        grammar_req_ids = grammar_output.structured_output_request_ids\n355\t\n356\t        if grammar_bitmask is None or len(grammar_req_ids) == 0:\n357\t            return logits\n358\t\n359\t        # Build mapping from request_id to bitmask index\n360\t        grammar_req_id_to_idx = {req_id: i for i, req_id in enumerate(grammar_req_ids)}\n361\t\n362\t        batch_size, vocab_size = logits.shape\n363\t        device = logits.device\n364\t        logits = logits.clone()\n365\t\n366\t        # For each request in the batch, find its bitmask (if any)\n367\t        for batch_idx, req_id in enumerate(self.input_batch.req_ids[:batch_size]):\n368\t            bitmask_idx = grammar_req_id_to_idx.get(req_id, -1)\n369\t\n370\t            if bitmask_idx == -1:\n371\t                # No grammar constraint for this request\n372\t                continue\n373\t\n374\t            # Get the bitmask for this request\n375\t            # grammar_bitmask is numpy array: [num_grammar_reqs, bitmask_size]\n376\t            req_bitmask = torch.from_numpy(grammar_bitmask[bitmask_idx]).to(device)\n377\t\n378\t            # Unpack and apply bitmask\n379\t            logits[batch_idx] = self._apply_packed_bitmask_to_row(\n380\t                logits[batch_idx], req_bitmask\n381\t            )\n382\t\n383\t        return logits\n384\t\n385\t    def _apply_packed_bitmask_to_row(\n386\t        self,\n387\t        logits_row: torch.Tensor,  # [vocab_size]\n388\t        packed_bitmask: torch.Tensor,  # [bitmask_size] int32\n389\t    ) -> torch.Tensor:\n390\t        """Apply packed bitmask to a single row of logits."""\n391\t        vocab_size = logits_row.shape[0]\n392\t        device = logits_row.device\n393\t\n394\t        # Unpack bitmask\n395\t        token_indices = torch.arange(vocab_size, device=device)\n396\t        word_indices = token_indices // 32\n397\t        bit_indices = token_indices % 32\n398\t\n399\t        # Clamp to bitmask size\n400\t        bitmask_size = packed_bitmask.shape[0]\n401\t        word_indices = word_indices.clamp(max=bitmask_size - 1)\n402\t\n403\t        # Get words and extract bits\n404\t        words = packed_bitmask[word_indices]\n405\t        bits = (words >> bit_indices) & 1\n406\t        valid_mask = bits.bool()\n407\t\n408\t        # Apply mask\n409\t        return logits_row.masked_fill(~valid_mask, float("-inf"))\n410\t\n411\t    def initialize_kv_cache(self, kv_cache_config: KVCacheConfig):\n412\t        """\n413\t        Initialize KV cache based on `kv_cache_config`.\n414\t        Args:\n415\t            kv_cache_config: Configuration for the KV cache, including the KV\n416\t            cache size of each layer\n417\t        """\n418\t        # For Neuron, we don\'t need to initialize kv cache memory space here as it is done\n419\t        # under the hood in NxD-I library. But we do need to register the kv cache space\n420\t        # for kv connector when has_kv_transfer_group() returns True.\n421\t\n422\t        if has_kv_transfer_group():\n423\t            nxdi_kv_cache_state = (\n424\t                self.model.model.context_encoding_model.model.nxd_model.state\n425\t            )\n426\t            kv_caches = {}\n427\t            logger.info("Registering host memory space")\n428\t            for rank, kv_on_tp_rank in enumerate(nxdi_kv_cache_state):\n429\t                # The NEURON_COMBINE_KV_ALLOCATIONS is exposed by the NxD library.\n430\t                # If enabled, it provides a merged view of a k tensor and its v tensor.\n431\t                # KV cache shape becomes (2, ...).\n432\t                if os.environ.get("NEURON_COMBINE_KV_ALLOCATIONS", "0") == "1":\n433\t                    logger.debug("Using combined kv allocations")\n434\t                    for key in kv_on_tp_rank:\n435\t                        # Filter only the `combined` KV tensors. Note the `combined` tensors\n436\t                        # are not tensor copy, but a view.\n437\t                        if key.startswith("kv_mgr.past_key_values.combined"):\n438\t                            layer = int(key.rsplit(".", 1)[-1])\n439\t                            kv_caches[f"tp{rank}_layer{layer}_kv"] = kv_on_tp_rank[key]\n440\t                else:\n441\t                    logger.debug("Using separate kv allocations")\n442\t                    # The vanilla NxDI kv state is a dict with the keys formulated as the following\n443\t                    # [\'kv_mgr.past_key_values.0\', \'kv_mgr.past_key_values.1\', ... ].\n444\t                    # where K tensor and V tensor are alternating.\n445\t\n446\t                    # Sort keys by numeric suffix so 0,1,2,3,... then loop through pairs of (0,1), (2,3)...\n447\t                    # so that we know if it is a K tensor or V tensor.\n448\t                    keys = sorted(\n449\t                        kv_on_tp_rank.keys(),\n450\t                        key=lambda name: int(name.rsplit(".", 1)[-1]),\n451\t                    )\n452\t                    if len(keys) % 2 != 0:\n453\t                        raise ValueError(\n454\t                            f"Uneven KV keys on tp rank {rank}: {len(keys)} keys"\n455\t                        )\n456\t                    for layer, (k_key, v_key) in enumerate(zip(keys[0::2], keys[1::2])):\n457\t                        kv_caches[f"tp{rank}_layer{layer}_k"] = kv_on_tp_rank[k_key]\n458\t                        kv_caches[f"tp{rank}_layer{layer}_v"] = kv_on_tp_rank[v_key]\n459\t\n460\t            get_kv_transfer_group().register_kv_caches(kv_caches)\n461\t\n462\t    def _get_nxdi_lora_config(self):\n463\t        """\n464\t        Neuron Multi-LoRA serving requires a json file to specify the available LoRA adapters\n465\t        on both device and CPU memory. The file is expected to pass via additional_config.override_neuron_config\n466\t        and the content is expected to be in the following format:\n467\t        {\n468\t            "lora-ckpt-dir": "/path/to/lora_adapter_dir",\n469\t            "lora-ckpt-paths": {\n470\t                "lora_id_1": "path/to/lora_adapter_1",\n471\t                "lora_id_2": "path/to/lora_adapter_2"\n472\t            },\n473\t            "lora-ckpt-paths-cpu": {\n474\t                "lora_id_1": "path/to/lora_adapter_1",\n475\t                "lora_id_2": "path/to/lora_adapter_2",\n476\t                "lora_id_3": "path/to/lora_adapter_3",\n477\t                "lora_id_4": "path/to/lora_adapter_4"\n478\t            }\n479\t        }\n480\t        """\n481\t        override_neuron_config = self.vllm_config.additional_config.get(\n482\t            "override_neuron_config", None\n483\t        )\n484\t        target_modules = override_neuron_config.pop("target_modules", None)\n485\t        lora_ckpt_json = override_neuron_config.pop("lora_ckpt_json", None)\n486\t        max_cpu_loras = self.lora_config.max_cpu_loras\n487\t        dynamic_multi_lora = (\n488\t            os.environ.get("VLLM_ALLOW_RUNTIME_LORA_UPDATING", "0") == "1"\n489\t            or max_cpu_loras > 0\n490\t        )\n491\t\n492\t        return LoraServingConfig(\n493\t            max_loras=self.lora_config.max_loras,\n494\t            max_lora_rank=self.lora_config.max_lora_rank,\n495\t            target_modules=target_modules,\n496\t            lora_ckpt_json=lora_ckpt_json,\n497\t            max_cpu_loras=max_cpu_loras,\n498\t            lora_memory_transpose=False,\n499\t            dynamic_multi_lora=dynamic_multi_lora,\n500\t            batch_size=self.scheduler_config.max_num_seqs,\n501\t            base_model_quantized=override_neuron_config.get("quantized", False),\n502\t            enable_base_model_only=True,\n503\t        )\n504\t\n505\t    def _get_last_token_position(self, state: CachedRequestState) -> int:\n506\t        """\n507\t        This is used to determine the position ID for the next decode step,\n508\t        where we process the last generated token.\n509\t\n510\t        Notes:\n511\t            - We calculate position id based on prompt len + total generated\n512\t            tokens (by draft and target model).\n513\t            - We do not use the request_data.num_computed_tokens from the\n514\t            scheduler output because that excludes speculated tokens.\n515\t            - This step is necessary to support Neuron\'s fused speculation feature.\n516\t\n517\t        Args:\n518\t            state: The cached request state containing token information.\n519\t\n520\t        Returns:\n521\t            int: The 0-indexed position of the last processed token.\n522\t        """\n523\t\n524\t        return len(state.prompt_token_ids) + len(state.output_token_ids) - 1\n525\t\n526\t    def load_model(self) -> None:\n527\t        # Update LoRA config\n528\t        lora_serving_config = None\n529\t        if self.lora_config is not None:\n530\t            lora_serving_config = self._get_nxdi_lora_config()\n531\t        with set_current_vllm_config(self.vllm_config):\n532\t            self.model = get_neuron_model(\n533\t                self.model_config,\n534\t                cache_config=self.cache_config,\n535\t                parallel_config=self.parallel_config,\n536\t                scheduler_config=self.scheduler_config,\n537\t                lora_serving_config=lora_serving_config,\n538\t                speculative_config=self.speculative_config,\n539\t                additional_config=self.vllm_config.additional_config,\n540\t            )\n541\t        if self.lora_config is not None:\n542\t            self.lora_manager = self.model.model.lora_model_manager\n543\t        self.model.is_reorder_needed = not (\n544\t            self.is_prefix_caching or self.is_chunked_prefill\n545\t        )\n546\t\n547\t        # Validate and log sampling configuration\n548\t        self._validate_sampling_configuration()\n549\t        self._validate_max_prompt_length()\n550\t\n551\t    def _validate_sampling_configuration(self) -> None:\n552\t        """\n553\t        Validate the sampling configuration and log the sampling strategy.\n554\t\n555\t        Raises:\n556\t            RuntimeError: If sampling configuration is invalid\n557\t        """\n558\t        try:\n559\t            has_on_device_sampling = (\n560\t                hasattr(self.model, "neuron_config")\n561\t                and hasattr(self.model.neuron_config, "on_device_sampling_config")\n562\t                and self.model.neuron_config.on_device_sampling_config is not None\n563\t            )\n564\t\n565\t            if has_on_device_sampling:\n566\t                logger.info(\n567\t                    "Hardware sampling enabled: config=%s",\n568\t                    self.model.neuron_config.on_device_sampling_config,\n569\t                )\n570\t                # Validate hardware sampling configuration\n571\t                config = self.model.neuron_config.on_device_sampling_config\n572\t                if hasattr(config, "global_topk") and (\n573\t                    config.global_topk <= 0\n574\t                    or config.global_topk > self._MAX_NEURON_SAMPLING_TOP_K\n575\t                ):\n576\t                    logger.warning(\n577\t                        "Hardware sampling global_topk=%s is outside the accepted range of [1-%s]. "\n578\t                        "Actual topk will be set to %s, the max for neuron.",\n579\t                        config.global_topk,\n580\t                        self._MAX_NEURON_SAMPLING_TOP_K,\n581\t                        self._MAX_NEURON_SAMPLING_TOP_K,\n582\t                    )\n583\t            else:\n584\t                logger.info(\n585\t                    "CPU sampling enabled: on_device_sampling_config is None. "\n586\t                    "All sampling will be performed on CPU using vLLM\'s standard sampler."\n587\t                )\n588\t\n589\t                # Ensure CPU sampler is available\n590\t                if not hasattr(self, "cpu_sampler") or self.cpu_sampler is None:\n591\t                    raise RuntimeError(\n592\t                        "CPU sampling is required but cpu_sampler is not initialized"\n593\t                    )\n594\t\n595\t            # Validate model has required sampling interface\n596\t            if not hasattr(self.model, "sample"):\n597\t                raise RuntimeError(\n598\t                    "Model does not have required \'sample\' method for hardware sampling"\n599\t                )\n600\t\n601\t        except Exception as e:\n602\t            logger.error("Sampling configuration validation failed: %s", str(e))\n603\t            raise RuntimeError("Invalid sampling configuration: %s" % str(e)) from e\n604\t\n605\t    def _validate_max_prompt_length(self) -> None:\n606\t        """\n607\t        Validate that the maximum prompt length configuration is consistent.\n608\t\n609\t        **Terminology clarification:**\n610\t\n611\t        There is a terminology mismatch between NxDI (Neuron) and vLLM:\n612\t\n613\t        - **NxDI/Neuron**: Uses `neuron_config.max_context_length` to specify the\n614\t        Maximum Prompt Length (MPL) - the longest prompt sequence the model accepts.\n615\t        This can differ from the model\'s total capacity.\n616\t\n617\t        - **vLLM**: Uses `max_model_len` or \'max_context_len` (MCL) to specify the model\'s total capacity.\n618\t        vLLM has no concept of distinguishing prompt tokens from output tokens. When validating input lengths,\n619\t        it treats all tokens the same regardless of whether they are part of the initial\n620\t        prompt or generated output tokens from previous iterations. Vllm also considers\n621\t        max_model_len and max_context_len (MCL) to be the same thing\n622\t\n623\t        To support Neuron models with MPL ≠ MCL, we expose `max_prompt_length` in\n624\t        vLLM\'s additional_config, which maps to Neuron\'s `neuron_config.max_context_length`.\n625\t\n626\t        **What this function does:**\n627\t\n628\t        Validates that if the user specifies `max_prompt_length` in\n629\t        `additional_config`, it matches the value configured in the Neuron model\'s\n630\t        `neuron_config.max_context_length`. This ensures the API server and\n631\t        model loader have consistent prompt length limits.\n632\t\n633\t        **Validation logic:**\n634\t\n635\t        - **If user provides `max_prompt_length`**: Validates it matches the\n636\t        neuron model\'s configuration. Raises error if mismatch.\n637\t\n638\t        - **If user does NOT provide `max_prompt_length`**: Issues a warning if the\n639\t        neuron model\'s max prompt length differs from vLLM\'s `max_model_len`,\n640\t        as this may cause server crashes.\n641\t\n642\t        Raises:\n643\t            RuntimeError: If user-provided `max_prompt_length` doesn\'t match the\n644\t                value in `neuron_config.max_context_length`.\n645\t\n646\t        Warns:\n647\t            If no `max_prompt_length` is provided and the neuron model\'s configured\n648\t            value differs from `max_model_len`.\n649\t        """\n650\t        neuron_config = self.model.neuron_config\n651\t\n652\t        def _get_max_prompt_len_from_neuron_config(neuron_config):\n653\t            if hasattr(neuron_config, "max_context_length"):\n654\t                return neuron_config.max_context_length\n655\t            # Bucketing case - find max bucket size\n656\t            if getattr(neuron_config, "enable_bucketing", False) and hasattr(\n657\t                neuron_config, "context_encoding_buckets"\n658\t            ):\n659\t                buckets = neuron_config.context_encoding_buckets\n660\t                return max(buckets) if buckets else None\n661\t\n662\t            return None\n663\t\n664\t        # mpl_value set in platform.py\n665\t        mpl_value = self.vllm_config.model_config.max_prompt_length\n666\t        mpl_nc_value = _get_max_prompt_len_from_neuron_config(neuron_config)\n667\t\n668\t        if mpl_value is None:\n669\t            if mpl_nc_value != self.max_model_len:\n670\t                logger.warning(\n671\t                    "Your Neuron model was compiled with max prompt length %s, "\n672\t                    "but max_model_len is set to %s. "\n673\t                    "To prevent the vLLM engine from crashing when prompts exceed %s tokens, "\n674\t                    \'add "max_prompt_length": %s to --additional-config when using the \'\n675\t                    "OpenAI API server. This will return a 400 error for oversized prompts instead of "\n676\t                    "terminating the engine. Alternatively, if you need to handle longer prompts, "\n677\t                    "you can recompile your Neuron model with a larger max_prompt_length by setting "\n678\t                    \'"max_context_length": %s in override_neuron_config when compiling.\',\n679\t                    mpl_nc_value,\n680\t                    self.max_model_len,\n681\t                    mpl_nc_value,\n682\t                    mpl_nc_value,\n683\t                    self.max_model_len,\n684\t                )\n685\t        else:\n686\t            if mpl_value != mpl_nc_value:\n687\t                raise RuntimeError(\n688\t                    f"Configuration mismatch: max_prompt_length in --additional-config ({mpl_value}) "\n689\t                    f"does not match the Neuron model\'s compiled max prompt length ({mpl_nc_value}). "\n690\t                    f\'Please update --additional-config to set "max_prompt_length": {mpl_nc_value}, \'\n691\t                    f"or recompile your Neuron model with the desired max prompt length by setting "\n692\t                    f\'"max_context_length": {mpl_value} in override_neuron_config when compiling.\'\n693\t                )\n694\t\n695\t        self.max_prompt_length = mpl_nc_value\n696\t\n697\t    @torch.inference_mode()\n698\t    def execute_model(\n699\t        self,\n700\t        scheduler_output: "SchedulerOutput",\n701\t        intermediate_tensors: IntermediateTensors | None = None,\n702\t    ) -> ModelRunnerOutput | None:\n703\t        """\n704\t        Execute model forward pass.\n705\t\n706\t        Always returns None to defer sampling to sample_tokens().\n707\t        """\n708\t        execute_start = time.perf_counter()\n709\t        batch_size = len(scheduler_output.scheduled_new_reqs) + len(\n710\t            scheduler_output.scheduled_cached_reqs.req_ids\n711\t        )\n712\t\n713\t        logger.debug("scheduler_output: %s", scheduler_output)\n714\t\n715\t        # Free slots of finished requests\n716\t        # We intentionally do this before updating the cached states as\n717\t        # the _update_states method is common across all hardware platforms.\n718\t        if self.use_custom_seq_id_mapping:\n719\t            for req_id in scheduler_output.finished_req_ids:\n720\t                if req_id in self.vllm_req_to_neuron_seq_id_mapping:\n721\t                    freed_slot = self.vllm_req_to_neuron_seq_id_mapping.pop(req_id)\n722\t                    self.free_seq_ids.add(freed_slot)\n723\t\n724\t        # Update cached state\n725\t        update_start = time.perf_counter()\n726\t        self._update_states(scheduler_output)\n727\t        update_elapsed = (time.perf_counter() - update_start) * 1000\n728\t        logger.debug("[PERF] _update_states: %.2fms", update_elapsed)\n729\t\n730\t        if not scheduler_output.total_num_scheduled_tokens:\n731\t            if not has_kv_transfer_group():\n732\t                # Return empty ModelRunnerOutput if there\'s no work to do.\n733\t                return EMPTY_MODEL_RUNNER_OUTPUT\n734\t\n735\t            return self.kv_connector_no_forward(scheduler_output, self.vllm_config)\n736\t\n737\t        # _prepare_model_input converts the scheduler output to ModelInputForNeuron\n738\t        prepare_start = time.perf_counter()\n739\t        model_input = self._prepare_model_input(scheduler_output)\n740\t        prepare_elapsed = (time.perf_counter() - prepare_start) * 1000\n741\t        logger.debug("[PERF] _prepare_model_input: %.2fms", prepare_elapsed)\n742\t\n743\t        logger.debug("model_input: %s", model_input)\n744\t\n745\t        # NOTE: setup current batch\'s metadata for kv connector.\n746\t        # Currently, only verified with NixlConnector\n747\t        with (\n748\t            set_forward_context(None, self.vllm_config),\n749\t            self.maybe_get_kv_connector_output(scheduler_output) as kv_connector_output,\n750\t        ):\n751\t            # Execute model forward pass (no sampling - deferred to sample_tokens())\n752\t            model_exec_start = time.perf_counter()\n753\t            if self.model.architecture in NEURON_MULTI_MODAL_MODELS:\n754\t                hidden_states = self._execute_model_for_multimodal_models(\n755\t                    model_input,\n756\t                    intermediate_tensors,\n757\t                )\n758\t            else:\n759\t                hidden_states = self._execute_model_for_text(\n760\t                    model_input,\n761\t                    intermediate_tensors,\n762\t                )\n763\t            model_exec_elapsed = (time.perf_counter() - model_exec_start) * 1000\n764\t            logger.debug("[PERF] model_execution: %.2fms", model_exec_elapsed)\n765\t\n766\t        # Store KV connector output for sample_tokens() to use\n767\t        self._kv_connector_output = kv_connector_output\n768\t\n769\t        # Cache for sample_tokens()\n770\t        self._cached_logits = hidden_states\n771\t        self._cached_model_input = model_input\n772\t\n773\t        total_elapsed = (time.perf_counter() - execute_start) * 1000\n774\t        logger.debug(\n775\t            "[PERF] execute_model total: %.2fms [batch=%d]", total_elapsed, batch_size\n776\t        )\n777\t\n778\t        # Return None to defer sampling to sample_tokens()\n779\t        return None\n780\t\n781\t    def _prepare_logits_for_sampling(\n782\t        self,\n783\t        hidden_states: torch.Tensor,\n784\t        model_input: ModelInputForNeuron,\n785\t    ) -> torch.Tensor:\n786\t        """\n787\t        Prepare logits for sampling.\n788\t        NOTE: For NxDI models without on-device sampling, the model forward\n789\t        pass should return logits directly (not hidden states).\n790\t        Verify your model configuration returns logits when\n791\t        on_device_sampling_config is None.\n792\t        """\n793\t        # Clone to avoid modifying model output tensor\n794\t        hidden_states = hidden_states.clone()\n795\t\n796\t        # Handle prefill completion state (mask incomplete prefills)\n797\t        if model_input.prefill_completion_state is not None:\n798\t            for i, state in enumerate(model_input.prefill_completion_state):\n799\t                if not state.item():\n800\t                    # This request\'s prefill isn\'t complete, mask its logits\n801\t                    hidden_states[i] = float("-inf")\n802\t\n803\t        # Reorder to match input batch order\n804\t        request_id_order = {\n805\t            request_id: idx for idx, request_id in enumerate(model_input.request_ids)\n806\t        }\n807\t\n808\t        reorder_indices = torch.tensor(\n809\t            [request_id_order[request_id] for request_id in self.input_batch.req_ids],\n810\t            dtype=torch.long,\n811\t            device=hidden_states.device,\n812\t        )\n813\t\n814\t        return hidden_states[reorder_indices]\n815\t\n816\t    def _generate_model_runner_output(\n817\t        self,\n818\t        sampler_outputs: SamplerOutput | None,\n819\t        kv_connector_output: KVConnectorOutput | None = None,\n820\t    ) -> ModelRunnerOutput:\n821\t        if sampler_outputs is None:\n822\t            return EMPTY_MODEL_RUNNER_OUTPUT\n823\t\n824\t        sampled_token_ids = sampler_outputs.sampled_token_ids\n825\t        spec_token_ids = None\n826\t\n827\t        if self.speculative_config is None:\n828\t            # No spec decode tokens.\n829\t            # Convert to list of Python int lists for vLLM scheduler compatibility\n830\t            # (vLLM\'s scheduler expects native Python ints, not numpy.int64)\n831\t            valid_sampled_token_ids = [\n832\t                [int(x) for x in row if x != -1] for row in sampled_token_ids.tolist()\n833\t            ]\n834\t\n835\t        else:\n836\t            # Modify NxDI output to conform to vLLM ModelRunnerOutput\n837\t            # sampled_token_ids: list[list[int]] (native Python ints)\n838\t            # spec_token_ids: Optional[list[list[int]]]\n839\t            # If NxDI returns [B, T, 1], squeeze the trailing dim.\n840\t            squeezed_tensor = (\n841\t                sampled_token_ids.squeeze(-1)\n842\t                if sampled_token_ids.dim() == 3 and sampled_token_ids.size(-1) == 1\n843\t                else sampled_token_ids\n844\t            )\n845\t\n846\t            # Work directly on tensor; only drop -1 pads (0 is a valid token).\n847\t            valid_sampled_token_ids = []\n848\t            spec_token_ids = []\n849\t            for row in squeezed_tensor.cpu():\n850\t                kept = [int(x) for x in row if x != -1]  # keep 0s; drop only -1 pads\n851\t                valid_sampled_token_ids.append(kept)\n852\t                spec_token_ids.append(kept[:-1] if kept else [])\n853\t                self.num_accepted_tokens += len(kept)\n854\t\n855\t            # Track total draft tokens proposed (speculation_length * batch_size)\n856\t            self.num_draft_tokens += squeezed_tensor.size(1) * squeezed_tensor.size(0)\n857\t\n858\t            # Log acceptance rate periodically\n859\t            if self.num_draft_tokens > 0 and self.num_draft_tokens % 500 == 0:\n860\t                acceptance_rate = self.num_accepted_tokens / self.num_draft_tokens\n861\t                logger.info(\n862\t                    "Speculative decoding metrics: acceptance_rate=%.3f, "\n863\t                    "accepted_tokens=%d, draft_tokens=%d",\n864\t                    acceptance_rate,\n865\t                    self.num_accepted_tokens,\n866\t                    self.num_draft_tokens,\n867\t                )\n868\t\n869\t            self.spec_token_ids = spec_token_ids\n870\t\n871\t        for req_idx, sampled_ids in enumerate(valid_sampled_token_ids):\n872\t            if len(sampled_ids) == 0:\n873\t                continue\n874\t\n875\t            start_idx = self.input_batch.num_tokens_no_spec[req_idx]\n876\t            end_idx = start_idx + len(sampled_ids)\n877\t            assert end_idx <= self.max_model_len, (\n878\t                "Sampled token IDs exceed the max model length. "\n879\t                f"Total number of tokens: {end_idx} > max_model_len: "\n880\t                f"{self.max_model_len}"\n881\t            )\n882\t\n883\t            # sampled_ids is already a list of native Python ints\n884\t            self.input_batch.token_ids_cpu[req_idx, start_idx:end_idx] = sampled_ids\n885\t            self.input_batch.num_tokens_no_spec[req_idx] = end_idx\n886\t            req_id = self.input_batch.req_ids[req_idx]\n887\t            req_state = self.requests[req_id]\n888\t            req_state.output_token_ids.extend(sampled_ids)\n889\t\n890\t        logger.debug("final valid_sampled_token_ids: %s", valid_sampled_token_ids)\n891\t\n892\t        logprobs = None\n893\t        if sampler_outputs.logprobs_tensors is not None:\n894\t            logprobs = sampler_outputs.logprobs_tensors.tolists()\n895\t\n896\t        return ModelRunnerOutput(\n897\t            req_ids=self.input_batch.req_ids,\n898\t            req_id_to_index=self.input_batch.req_id_to_index,\n899\t            sampled_token_ids=valid_sampled_token_ids,\n900\t            # CPU sampling supports logprobs.\n901\t            logprobs=logprobs,\n902\t            # TODO: support the following fields.\n903\t            prompt_logprobs_dict={},\n904\t            pooler_output=[],\n905\t            kv_connector_output=kv_connector_output,\n906\t        )\n907\t\n908\t    def get_kv_cache_spec(self) -> dict[str, KVCacheSpec]:\n909\t        """\n910\t        Generates the KVCacheSpec for Neuron models.\n911\t        Since Neuron uses compiled models without individual Attention layers,\n912\t        we manually create specs for each layer based on model config.\n913\t        Returns:\n914\t            KVCacheSpec: A dictionary mapping layer names to their KV cache\n915\t            format. Layers that do not need KV cache are not included.\n916\t        """\n917\t        # Get number of layers from model config\n918\t        num_layers = get_num_layers_from_hf_config(self.model_config.hf_config)\n919\t\n920\t        kv_cache_spec: dict[str, KVCacheSpec] = {}\n921\t\n922\t        # Create a spec for each layer\n923\t        for layer_idx in range(num_layers):\n924\t            layer_name = f"layers.{layer_idx}.self_attn"  # standard naming convention\n925\t            kv_cache_spec[layer_name] = FullAttentionSpec(\n926\t                block_size=self.block_size,\n927\t                num_kv_heads=self.parallel_config.tensor_parallel_size,\n928\t                head_size=self.model.head_dim,\n929\t                dtype=self.model_config.dtype,\n930\t                sliding_window=self.model_config.get_sliding_window(),\n931\t            )\n932\t\n933\t        return kv_cache_spec\n934\t\n935\t    def _update_states(self, scheduler_output: "SchedulerOutput") -> None:\n936\t        """Update the cached states and the persistent batch with the scheduler\n937\t        output.\n938\t\n939\t        The updated states are used by the `_prepare_inputs` function to create\n940\t        the input GPU tensors for the model.\n941\t\n942\t        The SamplingMetadata is updated and copied to the GPU if there is a\n943\t        new/resumed/paused/finished request in the batch.\n944\t        """\n945\t        # Remove finished requests from the cached states.\n946\t        for req_id in scheduler_output.finished_req_ids:\n947\t            self.requests.pop(req_id, None)\n948\t            if self.lora_config is not None:\n949\t                self.lora_manager.remove_req_id(req_id)\n950\t\n951\t        # Remove the finished requests from the persistent batch.\n952\t        # NOTE(woosuk): There could be an edge case where finished_req_ids and\n953\t        # scheduled_req_ids overlap. This happens when a request is aborted and\n954\t        # then resubmitted with the same ID. In this case, we treat them as two\n955\t        # distinct requests - clearing the cached states for the first request\n956\t        # and handling the second as a new request.\n957\t        for req_id in scheduler_output.finished_req_ids:\n958\t            self.input_batch.remove_request(req_id)\n959\t\n960\t        # Free the cached encoder outputs.\n961\t        for mm_hash in scheduler_output.free_encoder_mm_hashes:\n962\t            self.encoder_cache.pop(mm_hash, None)\n963\t\n964\t        # Remove the unscheduled requests from the persistent batch.\n965\t        # NOTE(woosuk): The unscheduled requests are either preempted requests\n966\t        # or running requests that are not scheduled in this step. We remove\n967\t        # them from the persistent batch but keep their cached states since\n968\t        # they will be scheduled again sometime in the future.\n969\t        scheduled_req_ids = scheduler_output.num_scheduled_tokens.keys()\n970\t        cached_req_ids = self.input_batch.req_id_to_index.keys()\n971\t        unscheduled_req_ids = cached_req_ids - scheduled_req_ids\n972\t        # NOTE(woosuk): The persistent batch optimization assumes that\n973\t        # consecutive batches contain mostly the same requests. If batches\n974\t        # have low request overlap (e.g., alternating between two distinct\n975\t        # sets of requests), this optimization becomes very inefficient.\n976\t        for req_id in unscheduled_req_ids:\n977\t            self.input_batch.remove_request(req_id)\n978\t\n979\t        reqs_to_add: list[CachedRequestState] = []\n980\t        # Add new requests to the cached states.\n981\t        for new_req_data in scheduler_output.scheduled_new_reqs:\n982\t            req_id = new_req_data.req_id\n983\t            sampling_params = new_req_data.sampling_params\n984\t            pooling_params = new_req_data.pooling_params\n985\t\n986\t            req_state = CachedRequestState(\n987\t                req_id=req_id,\n988\t                prompt_token_ids=new_req_data.prompt_token_ids,\n989\t                mm_features=new_req_data.mm_features or [],\n990\t                sampling_params=sampling_params,\n991\t                pooling_params=pooling_params,\n992\t                generator=None,\n993\t                block_ids=new_req_data.block_ids,\n994\t                num_computed_tokens=new_req_data.num_computed_tokens,\n995\t                output_token_ids=[],\n996\t                lora_request=new_req_data.lora_request,\n997\t            )\n998\t            self.requests[req_id] = req_state\n999\t\n1000\t            reqs_to_add.append(req_state)\n1001\t\n1002\t        # Update the states of the running/resumed requests.\n1003\t        req_data = scheduler_output.scheduled_cached_reqs\n1004\t        for i, req_id in enumerate(req_data.req_ids):\n1005\t            req_state = self.requests[req_id]\n1006\t            num_computed_tokens = req_data.num_computed_tokens[i]\n1007\t            new_block_ids = req_data.new_block_ids[i]\n1008\t            resumed_from_preemption = req_id in req_data.resumed_req_ids\n1009\t\n1010\t            # Update the cached states.\n1011\t            req_state.num_computed_tokens = self._get_last_token_position(req_state)\n1012\t\n1013\t            # Update the block IDs.\n1014\t            if not resumed_from_preemption:\n1015\t                if new_block_ids is not None:\n1016\t                    # Append the new blocks to the existing block IDs.\n1017\t                    for block_ids, new_ids in zip(req_state.block_ids, new_block_ids):\n1018\t                        block_ids.extend(new_ids)\n1019\t            else:\n1020\t                assert new_block_ids is not None\n1021\t                # The request is resumed from preemption.\n1022\t                # Replace the existing block IDs with the new ones.\n1023\t                req_state.block_ids = new_block_ids\n1024\t\n1025\t            req_index = self.input_batch.req_id_to_index.get(req_id)\n1026\t            if req_index is None:\n1027\t                # The request is not in the persistent batch.\n1028\t                # The request was either preempted and resumed later, or was not\n1029\t                # scheduled in the previous step and needs to be added again.\n1030\t                reqs_to_add.append(req_state)\n1031\t                continue\n1032\t\n1033\t            # Update the persistent batch.\n1034\t            self.input_batch.num_computed_tokens_cpu[req_index] = num_computed_tokens\n1035\t            if new_block_ids is not None:\n1036\t                self.input_batch.block_table.append_row(new_block_ids, req_index)\n1037\t\n1038\t            # Add spec_token_ids to token_ids_cpu.\n1039\t            spec_token_ids = scheduler_output.scheduled_spec_decode_tokens.get(\n1040\t                req_id, ()\n1041\t            )\n1042\t            if spec_token_ids:\n1043\t                num_spec_tokens = len(spec_token_ids)\n1044\t                start_index = self.input_batch.num_tokens_no_spec[req_index]\n1045\t                end_token_index = start_index + num_spec_tokens\n1046\t                self.input_batch.token_ids_cpu[\n1047\t                    req_index, start_index:end_token_index\n1048\t                ] = spec_token_ids\n1049\t                # NOTE(woosuk): `num_tokens` here may include spec tokens.\n1050\t                self.input_batch.num_tokens_no_spec[req_index] += num_spec_tokens\n1051\t\n1052\t        # Add the new or resumed requests to the persistent batch.\n1053\t        # The smaller empty indices are filled first.\n1054\t        for request in reqs_to_add:\n1055\t            self.input_batch.add_request(request)\n1056\t\n1057\t        # Condense the batched states if there are gaps left by removed requests\n1058\t        self.input_batch.condense()\n1059\t        # Allow attention backend to reorder the batch, potentially\n1060\t        # self._may_reorder_batch(scheduler_output)\n1061\t        # Refresh batch metadata with any pending updates.\n1062\t        self.input_batch.refresh_metadata()\n1063\t\n1064\t    def _execute_model_for_text(\n1065\t        self,\n1066\t        model_input: ModelInputForNeuron,\n1067\t        intermediate_tensors: IntermediateTensors | None = None,\n1068\t    ) -> torch.Tensor:\n1069\t        """Execute model forward pass for text models.\n1070\t\n1071\t        Returns:\n1072\t            hidden_states: Model output tensor\n1073\t        """\n1074\t        hidden_states = self.model(\n1075\t            input_ids=model_input.input_tokens,\n1076\t            position_ids=model_input.position_ids,\n1077\t            input_block_ids=model_input.input_block_ids,\n1078\t            slot_mapping=model_input.slot_mapping,\n1079\t            block_tables=model_input.block_tables,\n1080\t            full_context_lens=model_input.full_context_lens,\n1081\t            computed_context_lens=model_input.computed_context_lens,\n1082\t            sampling_params=model_input.sampling_params,\n1083\t            adapter_ids=model_input.adapter_ids,\n1084\t            prefill_completion_state=model_input.prefill_completion_state,\n1085\t            **_mm_kwargs_to_device(model_input.multi_modal_kwargs, self.device),\n1086\t        )\n1087\t        return hidden_states\n1088\t\n1089\t    def _execute_model_for_multimodal_models(\n1090\t        self,\n1091\t        model_input: ModelInputForNeuron,\n1092\t        intermediate_tensors: IntermediateTensors | None = None,\n1093\t    ) -> torch.Tensor:\n1094\t        """Execute model forward pass for multimodal models.\n1095\t\n1096\t        Returns:\n1097\t            hidden_states: Model output tensor\n1098\t        """\n1099\t        hidden_states = self.model.execute_model(model_input)\n1100\t        return hidden_states\n1101\t\n1102\t    def _process_multi_modal_data_neuron(\n1103\t        self, mm_data: list[MultiModalFeatureSpec]\n1104\t    ) -> BatchedTensorInputs:\n1105\t        if len(mm_data) == 1:\n1106\t            mm_item = mm_data[0].data  # Type: Optional[MultiModalKwargsItem]\n1107\t            # Get tensor data from MultiModalKwargsItem\n1108\t            if mm_item is None:\n1109\t                mm_kwargs: dict[str, NestedTensors] = {}\n1110\t            else:\n1111\t                mm_kwargs = mm_item.get_data()\n1112\t        elif len(mm_data) > 1:\n1113\t            mm_kwargs = {}\n1114\t            for mm_item in mm_data:  # Type: List[MultiModalFeatureSpec]\n1115\t                for k, v in mm_item.data.items():\n1116\t                    if k not in mm_kwargs:\n1117\t                        mm_kwargs[k] = []\n1118\t                    mm_kwargs[k].append(v.data)\n1119\t\n1120\t        logger.debug("mm_data in _process_multi_modal_data_neuron: %s", mm_kwargs)\n1121\t\n1122\t        if self.model.model.config.model_type == "llava":\n1123\t            mm_kwargs = self._process_multi_modal_data_neuron_llava(mm_kwargs)\n1124\t        elif self.model.model.config.model_type == "qwen2_vl":\n1125\t            mm_kwargs = self._process_multi_modal_data_neuron_qwen2_vl(mm_kwargs)\n1126\t        elif self.model.model.config.model_type == "qwen3_vl":\n1127\t            # Qwen3-VL uses the same processing as Qwen2-VL\n1128\t            mm_kwargs = self._process_multi_modal_data_neuron_qwen2_vl(mm_kwargs)\n1129\t        elif self.model.model.config.model_type == "llama4":\n1130\t            pass  # llama4 doesn\'t require special processing\n1131\t        else:\n1132\t            raise NotImplementedError(\n1133\t                f"processing mm data for model type {self.model.model.config.model_type} not supported on Neuron yet!"\n1134\t            )\n1135\t\n1136\t        return mm_kwargs\n1137\t\n1138\t    def _process_multi_modal_data_neuron_llava(self, mm_data):\n1139\t        # We reconstruct image_sizes here to match HF\'s implementation\n1140\t        # since vLLM implementation slices pixel_values for each image separately\n1141\t        # (see vllm/model_executor/models/llava.py)\n1142\t        if isinstance(mm_data["pixel_values"], torch.Tensor):\n1143\t            logger.debug("pixel_values tensor shape: %s", mm_data["pixel_values"].shape)\n1144\t            pixel_values = mm_data["pixel_values"]\n1145\t            # Ensure pixel_values is 4D [B, C, H, W]\n1146\t            # vLLM may pass 3D [C, H, W] for single images\n1147\t            if pixel_values.dim() == 3:\n1148\t                pixel_values = pixel_values.unsqueeze(0)\n1149\t                mm_data["pixel_values"] = pixel_values\n1150\t                logger.debug("Added batch dimension, new shape: %s", pixel_values.shape)\n1151\t            # Now pixel_values is 4D [B, C, H, W]\n1152\t            img_height = pixel_values.shape[2]\n1153\t            img_width = pixel_values.shape[3]\n1154\t            # image_sizes must be 2D [[height, width]] for NxDI patchify\n1155\t            mm_data["image_sizes"] = torch.tensor(\n1156\t                [[img_height, img_width]], dtype=torch.int32\n1157\t            )\n1158\t        elif isinstance(mm_data["pixel_values"], list):\n1159\t            image_sizes_list = []\n1160\t            # The below logic pads multiple images within one request to\n1161\t            # max height and width across all images\n1162\t            # This mimics the same logic as HF processor\n1163\t            max_height = 0\n1164\t            max_width = 0\n1165\t            for pixel_values in mm_data["pixel_values"]:\n1166\t                logger.debug("pixel_values.shape: %s", pixel_values.shape)\n1167\t                # vLLM may pass 3D [C, H, W] for each image\n1168\t                if pixel_values.dim() == 3:\n1169\t                    pixel_values = pixel_values.unsqueeze(0)\n1170\t                    logger.debug(\n1171\t                        "Added batch dimension, new shape: %s", pixel_values.shape\n1172\t                    )\n1173\t                img_height = pixel_values.shape[2]\n1174\t                img_width = pixel_values.shape[3]\n1175\t                max_height = max(max_height, img_height)\n1176\t                max_width = may pass 3D [C, H, W] for each image\n1184\t                if pixel_values.dim() == 3:\n1185\t                    pixel_values = pixel_values.unsqueeze(0)\n1186\t                    logger.debug(\n1187\t                        "Added batch dimension, new shape: %s", pixel_values.shape\n1188\t                    )\n1189\t                img_height = pixel_values.shape[2]\n1190\t                img_width = pixel_values.shape[3]\n1191\t                padded_pixel_value = torch.nn.functional.pad(\n1192\t                    pixel_values,\n1193\t                    (0, max_width - img_width, 0, max_height - img_height),\n1194\t                    value=0,\n1195\t                )\n1196\t                logger.debug("padded_pixel_value shape: %s",       logger.debug("mm_data in _process_multi_modal_data_neuron_llava: %s", mm_data)\n1200\t        return mm_data\n1201\t\n1202\t    def _process_multi_modal_data_neuron_qwen2_vl(self,        if isinstance(pixel_values, list):\n1208\t            mm_data["pixel_values"] = torch.cat(pixel_values, dim=0)\n1209\t\n1210\t        image_grid_thw = mm_data\n1222\t\n1223\t    def _prepare_model_input(\n1224\t        self,\n1225\t        scheduler_output: "SchedulerOutput",\n1226\t    ) -> ModelInputForNeuron:\n1227\t        if _prepare_chunked_prefill_inputs(\n1250\t        self,\n1251\t        scheduler_output: "SchedulerOutput",\n1252\t    ) -> IntermediateInputData:\n1253\t        """\n1254\t        This function is used to prepare the inputs for chunked prefill.\n1255\t        It needs to treat prefill and decoding requests differently.\n1256\t          *  For NewRequestData, it is guaranteed to be a prefill request.\n1257\t          *  For CachedRequestData, it can be a prefill request or a decoding request.\n1258\t          The way to tell if it is a prefill request is to check if the number of\n1259\t          computed tokens is less than the number of context tokens.\n1260\t        """\n1261\t        data = IntermediateInputData()\n1262\t        num_scheduled_tokens = scheduler_output.num_scheduled_tokens\n1263\t        logger.debug("num_scheduled_tokens: %s", num_scheduled_tokens)\n1264\t\n1265\t        for request_data in scheduler_output.scheduled_new_reqs:\n1266\t            self._process_new_request_for_chunked_prefill(\n1267\t                request_data, num_scheduled_tokens[request_data.req_id], data\n1268\t            )\n1269\t\n1270\t        cached_request_data = scheduler_output.scheduled_cached_reqs\n1271\t        for i, req_id in enumerate(cached_request_data.req_ids):\n1272\t            self._process_cached_request_for_chunked_prefill(\n1273\t                cached_request_data, i, num_scheduled_tokens[req_id], data\n1274\t            )\n1275\t\n1276\t        return data\n1277\t\n1278\t    def _prepare_continuous_batching_inputs(\n1279\t        self,\n1280\t        scheduler_output: "SchedulerOutput",\n1281\t    ) -> Tuple[IntermediateInputData, bool]:\n1282\t        """\n1283\t        This function is used to prepare the inputs for continuous batching.\n1284\t            For NewRequestData,\n1285\t                1. On decode nodes in the DI setting, it should always do decoding.\n1286\t                2. For all other cases (i.e., prefill nodes in DI, non-DI case), do\n1287\t                   prefills.\n1288\t            For CachedRequestData, it is guaranteed to be a decoding request.\n1289\t        """\n1290\t        data = IntermediateInputData()\n1291\t        is_prefill = False\n1292\t        for request_data in scheduler_output.scheduled_new_reqs:\n1293\t            if (\n1294\t                scheduler_output.kv_connector_metadata is not None\n1295\t                and not scheduler_output.kv_connector_metadata.reqs_to_save\n1296\t            ):\n1297\t                # This branch is activated only if the current node is a decode node in the DI setting.\n1298\t                # 1. we cannot use `request_data.num_computed_tokens > 0` to indicate the node is decode because\n1299\t                # prefill with APC can also lead to request_data.num_computed_tokens > 0\n1300\t                # 2. we cannot use `scheduler_output.kv_connector_metadata.reqs_to_recv is not None` because on decode node,\n1301\t                # the scheduler always schedules transfer before scheduling decode for a request. So the scheduler output\n1302\t                # for the new decode request has empty reqs_to_recv.\n1303\t\n1304\t                logger.debug("Prepare model input for decoding for the new request")\n1305\t                self._process_new_request_for_disaggregated_inference(\n1306\t                    request_data, data\n1307\t                )\n1308\t                is_prefill = False\n1309\t            else:\n1310\t                self._process_new_request_for_continuous_batching(request_data, data)\n1311\t                is_prefill = True\n1312\t\n1313\t        cached_request_data = scheduler_output.scheduled_cached_reqs\n1314\t        for i, req_id in enumerate(cached_request_data.req_ids):\n1315\t            self._process_cached_request_for_continuous_batching(\n1316\t                cached_request_data, i, data\n1317\t            )\n1318\t\n1319\t        return data, is_prefill\n1320\t\n1321\t    def _process_new_request_for_continuous_batching(\n1322\t        self, request_data: NewRequestData, data: IntermediateInputData\n1323\t    ) -> None:\n1324\t        # Assign a free sequence id to the new request.\n1325\t        assert request_data.req_id not in self.vllm_req_to_neuron_seq_id_mapping, (\n1326\t            "Encountered an existing request ID while prefilling a new request"\n1327\t        )\n1328\t        assert self.free_seq_ids, "No free sequence ID available!"\n1329\t        assigned_slot = self.free_seq_ids.pop()\n1330\t        self.vllm_req_to_neuron_seq_id_mapping[request_data.req_id] = assigned_slot\n1331\t\n1332\t        data.request_ids.append(request_data.req_id)\n1333\t\n1334\t        data.input_tokens.append(request_data.prompt_token_ids)\n1335\t        if len(request_data.prompt_token_ids) > self.max_prompt_length:\n1336\t            raise ValueError(\n1337\t                f"Prompt length ({len(request_data.prompt_token_ids)} tokens) exceeds the maximum "\n1338\t                f"prompt length ({self.max_prompt_length} tokens) for this Neuron model. "\n1339\t                f\'To handle this gracefully during online serving, add "max_prompt_length": \'\n1340\t                f"{self.max_prompt_length} to --additional-config.     data.multi_modal_kwargs = self._process_multi_modal_data_neuron(\n1360\t                request_data.mm_features\n1361\t            )\n1362\t\n1363\t    def _process_new_request_for_continuous_batching_with_prefix_caching(\n1364\t        self, request_data: NewRequestData, data: IntermediateInputData\n1365\t    ) -> None:\n1366\t        assert block_size = self.cache_config.block_size\n1371\t        max_len = self.model_config.max_model_len\n1372\t        max_blocks_per_seq = max_len // block_size\n1373\t        padded_block_table = _process_new_request_for_disaggregated_inference(\n1391\t        self, request_data: NewRequestData, data: IntermediateInputData\n1392\t    ) -> None:\n1393\t        """\n1394\t        This method _process_cached_request_for_continuous_batching_with_prefix_caching(\n1469\t        self, request_data: CachedRequestData, index: int, data: IntermediateInputData\n1470\t    ) -> None:\n1471\t [{'tool_use_id': 'toolu_bdrk_01RKJp9Pes6t4xgRm5RBtcoL', 'type': 'tool_result', 'content': '1\t# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0\n2\timport logging\n3\tfrom collections import deque\n4\tfrom typing import TYPE_CHECKING\n5\t\n6\tfrom vllm.v1.core.sched.scheduler import Scheduler\n7\tfrom vllm.v1.core.sched.utils import check_stop\n8\tfrom vllm.v1.request import Request\n9\t\n10\tif TYPE_CHECKING:\n11\t    from vllm.v1.core.sched.output import SchedulerOutput\n12\telse:\n13\t    SchedulerOutput = None\n14\t\n15\tlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n16\tlogger.setLevel(logging.INFO)\n17\t\n18\t\n19\tclass NeuronScheduler(Scheduler):\n20\t    """Base class inheriting from the V1 scheduler to support continuous\n21\t    batching respecting Neuron constraints."""\n22\t\n23\t    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs) -> None:\n24\t        # Initialize vLLM scheduler\n25\t        super().__init__(*args, **kwargs)\n26\t\n27\t        # Requests are temporarily moved to this queue so that the base\n28\t        # scheduler does not see them. This lets us ensure that the set of\n29\t        # requests scheduled have at least one common warmup shape.\n30\t        self.holdback_queue: deque[Request] = deque()\n31\t\n32\t    def _update_request_with_output(\n33\t        self,\n34\t        request: Request,\n35\t        new_token_ids: list[int],\n36\t    ) -> tuple[list[int], bool]:\n37\t        """\n38\t        Override to prevent assertion crash during speculative decoding.\n39\t\n40\t        Issue: When using EAGLE/speculative decoding near max_model_len,\n41\t        the draft model adds extra tokens that can exceed max_model_len,\n42\t        causing \'Sampled token IDs exceed the max model length\' assertion.\n43\t\n44\t        Fix: Stop generation at (max_model_len - num_spec_tokens) to leave\n45\t        room for speculative tokens.\n46\t        """\n47\t        stopped = False\n48\t        spec_len = getattr(self, "num_spec_tokens", 0)\n49\t        effective_max_len = max(self.max_model_len - spec_len, 0)\n50\t\n51\t        for num_new, output_token_id in enumerate(new_token_ids, 1):\n52\t            request.append_output_token_ids(output_token_id)\n53\t\n54\t            stopped = check_stop(request, effective_max_len)\n55\t            if stopped:\n56\t                del new_token_ids[num_new:]\n57\t                break\n58\t        return new_token_ids, stopped\n59\t\n60\t\n61\tclass ContinuousBatchingNeuronScheduler(NeuronScheduler):\n62\t    """Support of continuous batching"""\n63\t\n64\t    # inherited from V1 base scheduler but mypy needs to know the type\n65\t    running: list[Request]\n66\t\n67\t    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs) -> None:\n68\t        # Initialize NeuronScheduler\n69\t        super().__init__(*args, **kwargs)\n70\t\n71\t    def schedule(self) -> "SchedulerOutput":\n72\t        """This override adds constraints and then delegates most of the work\n73\t        to the base scheduler\n74\t\n75\t        To avoid additional specialization, some requests are held back from the\n76\t        base scheduler but are restored after.\n77\t        """\n78\t\n79\t        # First purge the full waiting queue into our holdback queue, preserving\n80\t        # priority\n81\t        while self.waiting:\n82\t            self.holdback_queue.append(self.waiting.popleft())\n83\t\n84\t        # Check if new requests can be scheduled.\n85\t        while self.holdback_queue:\n86\t            if self.can_schedule(self.holdback_queue[0]):\n87\t                # Add request to the waiting queue\n88\t                self.waiting.append(self.holdback_queue.popleft())\n89\t            else:\n90\t                # Otherwise, we simply stop here so that the scheduler\n91\t                # can work with the batch we have\n92\t                break\n93\t\n94\t        # Schedule Prefill and Decode separately\n95\t        if len(self.waiting) > 0:\n96\t            # running and waiting queues are both empty -> start new batch\n123\t        start_new_batch = len(self.running) + len(self.waiting) == 0\n124\t        # check that there is space in the current decode batch\n125\t        cond1 = len(self.running) + len(self.waiting) < self.max_num_running_reqs\n126\t        # accuracy.\n126\t\n127\t        TODO: This sequence id reordering is better to live in NxD-Inference.\n128\t        """\n129\t        logger.debug("is_reorder_needed: %s",
