        sort_elapsed = (time.perf_counter() - sort_start) * 1000\n134\t            logger.debug("[PERF]       torch.sort: %.2fms", sort_elapsed)\n135\t\n136\t            sort_inputs_start = time.perf_counter()\n137\t            reordered_inputs = self._sort_inputs(inputs, sorted_indices)\n138\t            sort_inputs_elapsed = (time.perf_counter() - sort_inputs_start) * 1000\n139\t            logger.debug("[PERF]       _sort_inputs: %.2fms", sort_inputs_elapsed)\n140\t\n141\t            def restore(output: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:\n142\t                if sorted_ids.shape[0] != 1:\n143\t                    return torch.index_select(output, 0, torch.argsort(sorted_indices))\n144\t                return output\n145\t\n146\t            yield sorted_ids, reordered_inputs, restore\n147\t        else:\n148\t            yield input_block_ids, inputs, lambda x: x\n149\t\n150\t    @staticmethod\n151\t    def _sort_inputs(\n152\t        inputs: dict[str, Any], sorted_indices: torch.Tensor\n153\t    ) -> dict[str, Any]:\n154\t        """Apply sorting to a dict of tensor/list inputs along batch dimension."""\n155\t        sorted_inputs = {}\n156\t        for k, v in inputs.items():\n157\t            if isinstance(v, torch.Tensor):\n158\t                if v.shape[0] > 0:  # avoid empty tensors\n159\t                    if (\n160\t                        v.shape[0] != sorted_indices.shape[0]\n161\t                    ):  # mm inputs are only sorted during prefill\n162\t                        logger.debug(\n163\t                            "Skipping reorder for key %s which has batch size %s but sorted_indices has len %s",\n164\t                            k,\n165\t                            v.shape[0],\n166\t                            sorted_indices.shape[0],\n167\t                        )\n168\t                        sorted_inputs[k] = v\n169\t                        continue\n170\t                    sorted_inputs[k] = torch.index_select(v, 0, sorted_indices)\n171\t                else:\n172\t                    sorted_inputs[k] = v\n173\t            elif isinstance(v, list):\n174\t                sorted_inputs[k] = [v[i.item()] for i in sorted_indices]\n175\t            else:\n176\t                sorted_inputs[k] = v\n177\t        return sorted_inputs\n178\t\n179\t    def _load_weights_common(\n180\t        self, model_name_or_path: str, neuronx_model_cls, **kwargs\n181\t    ):\n182\t        # ===== Extract draft-specific config BEFORE creating any NeuronConfig =====\n183\t        neuron_config_dict = kwargs["neuron_config"]\n184\t        draft_overrides = neuron_config_dict.pop("draft_overrides", None)\n185\t        # ===== END EXTRACTION =====\n186\t\n187\t        neuron_config = neuronx_model_cls.get_neuron_config_cls()(**neuron_config_dict)\n188\t\n189\t        config = kwargs.get("config") or neuronx_model_cls.get_config_cls()(\n190\t            neuron_config, load_config=load_pretrained_config(model_name_or_path)\n191\t        )\n192\t\n193\t        # If fused speculation is enabled, attach the draft model config.\n194\t        if getattr(neuron_config, "enable_fused_speculation", False):\n195\t            assert kwargs.get("speculative_config") is not None, (\n196\t                "Must pass speculative_config to load weights if using Neuron Speculation."\n197\t            )\n198\t            self._init_fused_spec_config(\n199\t                config,\n200\t                neuron_config_dict,  # Already cleaned\n201\t                neuronx_model_cls,\n202\t                kwargs["speculative_config"],\n203\t                draft_overrides,\n204\t            )\n205\t        hashed_config = hashlib.md5(config.to_json_string().encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()\n206\t        compiled_model_path = self._get_compiled_model_path(\n207\t            model_name_or_path, hashed_config\n208\t        )\n209\t\n210\t        try:\n211\t            self._load_compiled_model(compiled_model_path, neuronx_model_cls, kwargs)\n212\t            return True, compiled_model_path, config\n213\t        except (FileNotFoundError, ValueError) as e:\n214\t            logger.warning("Exception: %s", e)\n215\t            logger.warning(\n216\t                "Unable to find precompiled artifacts from %s. Recompiling...",\n217\t                compiled_model_path,\n218\t            )\n219\t            return False, compiled_model_path, config\n220\t\n221\t    def _get_compiled_model_path(self, model_name_or_path: str, hashed_config: str):\n222\t        if os.getenv("NEURON_COMPILED_ARTIFACTS"):\n223\t            return os.getenv("NEURON_COMPILED_ARTIFACTS")\n224\t        elif os.path.exists(model_name_or_path):\n225\t            path = (\n226\t                Path(model_name_or_path) / "neuron-compiled-artifacts" / hashed_config\n227\t            )\n228\t            path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n229\t            shutil.rmtree(path, ignore_errors=True)\n230\t            return path\n231\t        else:\n232\t            path = (\n233\t                Path("local-models")\n234\t                / model_name_or_path\n235\t                / "neuron-compiled-artifacts"\n236\t                / hashed_config\n237\t            )\n238\t            path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n239\t            shutil.rmtree(path, ignore_errors=True)\n240\t            return path\n241\t\n242\t    def _load_compiled_model(self, compiled_model_path: str, neuronx_model_cls, kwargs):\n243\t        self.model = neuronx_model_cls(compiled_model_path)\n244\t\n245\t        self.model.load(compiled_model_path)\n246\t        logger.info(\n247\t            "Successfully loaded pre-compiled model artifacts from %s",\n248\t            compiled_model_path,\n249\t        )\n250\t        # When loading a pre-compiled model don\'t do any more overrides.\n251\t        override_neuron_config = kwargs.get("override_neuron_config")\n252\t        if override_neuron_config:\n253\t            logger.warning(\n254\t                "Using pre-compiled artifacts, override_neuron_config will be ignored"\n255\t            )\n256\t\n257\t    def _save_pretrained_model(self, model_name: str):\n258\t        hf_model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(model_name)\n259\t        saved_path = os.path.join("local-models", model_name)\n260\t        hf_model.save_pretrained(saved_path)\n261\t        return saved_path\n262\t\n263\t    def _compile_and_load_model(\n264\t        self, model_path: str, neuronx_model_cls, config, compiled_path: str\n265\t    ):\n266\t        self.model = neuronx_model_cls(model_path, config)\n267\t        # Quantize model.\n268\t        if config.neuron_config.quantized:\n269\t            neuronx_model_cls.save_quantized_state_dict(model_path, config)\n270\t        self.model.compile(compiled_path)\n271\t        self.model.load(compiled_path)\n272\t\n273\t    def _init_fused_spec_config(\n274\t        self,\n275\t        config,\n276\t        neuron_config_dict,\n277\t        neuronx_model_cls,\n278\t        speculative_config,\n279\t        draft_overrides=None,\n280\t    ):\n281\t        """\n282\t        Initialize and attach a `fused_spec_config` to the target model\'s\n283\t        NeuronXDistributed config when fused speculation is enabled.\n284\t\n285\t        Supports both homogeneous (same architecture) and heterogeneous\n286\t        (different architectures) draft models via automatic architecture detection.\n287\t\n288\t        Behavior:\n289\t        • Deep copy the target\'s instantiated `neuron_config` object to\n290\t        build draft config (preserves all fields without manual filtering).\n291\t        • Force-disable `enable_fused_speculation` in the draft to prevent\n292\t        recursion (only the target should run fused speculation).\n293\t        • Zero out `speculation_length` for the draft unless EAGLE is used,\n294\t        since the target controls speculation length.\n295\t        • Apply `draft_model_modules_to_not_convert` if specified.\n296\t        • For EAGLE drafts, mark `is_eagle_draft=True`.\n297\t        • Apply user-provided `draft_overrides` as attributes to handle\n298\t        architecture differences (e.g., different hidden sizes, kernels).\n299\t        • Auto-detect draft model class from checkpoint\'s config.json.\n300\t        • Load the draft HF config and wrap everything in a\n301\t        `FusedSpecNeuronConfig`, which is then attached to the target\'s config.\n302\t\n303\t        Draft Model Class Resolution:\n304\t            1. Auto-detect from draft checkpoint\'s config.json `architectures` field\n305\t            2. Fallback to target model class if detection fails (homogeneous speculation)\n306\t\n307\t        Args:\n308\t            config: The target model\'s NxDI config (will be modified in place\n309\t                    to attach `fused_spec_config`).\n310\t            neuron_config_dict: Original neuron configuration dictionary from\n311\t                    vLLM\'s `override_neuron_config` (used to extract draft settings).\n312\t            neuronx_model_cls: The NxDI model class for the target model, providing\n313\t                    config loaders. Used as draft class if auto-detection fails.\n314\t            speculative_config: vLLM\'s `SpeculativeConfig` describing the draft\n315\t                    model path and speculation parameters.\n316\t            draft_overrides: Optional dict of draft-specific config overrides applied\n317\t                    as attributes. Use to specify architecture differences (e.g.,\n318\t                    `{"padded_intermediate_size": 14336, "mlp_kernel_enabled": True}`).\n319\t                    Only specify fields that differ from target.\n320\t\n321\t        Raises:\n322\t            ValueError: If draft config cannot be loaded from checkpoint.\n323\t\n324\t        Notes:\n325\t            Only the *target* model should have\n326\t            `neuron_config.enable_fused_speculation=True`. The draft must not,\n327\t            otherwise NxDI would attempt to compile nested fused speculation.\n328\t\n329\t            Configuration inheritance: Draft inherits ALL target fields via deep copy,\n330\t            then selectively overrides specific fields via `draft_overrides`.\n331\t        """\n332\t        # ===== KEY: Deep copy the CREATED target neuron_config object =====\n333\t        # This preserves all target-specific fields without needing to filter\n334\t        draft_neuron_config = copy.deepcopy(config.neuron_config)\n335\t\n336\t        # Modify specific draft attributes (reference pattern)\n337\t        if not getattr(config.neuron_config, "enable_eagle_speculation", False):\n338\t            draft_neuron_config.speculation_length = 0\n339\t\n340\t        draft_neuron_config.enable_fused_speculation = False\n341\t\n342\t        if getattr(config.neuron_config, "draft_model_modules_to_not_convert", None):\n343\t            draft_neuron_config.modules_to_not_convert = (\n344\t                config.neuron_config.draft_model_modules_to_not_convert\n345\t            )\n346\t\n347\t        if getattr(config.neuron_config, "enable_eagle_speculation", False):\n348\t            draft_neuron_config.is_eagle_draft = True\n349\t\n350\t        # Apply draft overrides as attributes (not dict update)\n351\t        if draft_overrides:\n352\t            for key, value in draft_overrides.items():\n353\t                setattr(draft_neuron_config, key, value)\n354\t\n355\t        # ===== Load draft config for architecture inspection =====\n356\t        logger.info("Inspecting draft model config from: %s", speculative_config.model)\n357\t        try:\n358\t            from transformers import AutoConfig\n359\t\n360\t            draft_hf_config_for_inspection = AutoConfig.from_pretrained(\n361\t                speculative_config.model, trust_remote_code=False\n362\t            )\n363\t            logger.debug(\n364\t                "Draft config architectures: %s",\n365\t                getattr(draft_hf_config_for_inspection, "architectures", None),\n366\t            )\n367\t        except Exception as e:\n368\t            logger.error("Failed to load draft config for inspection: %s", e)\n369\t            raise ValueError(\n370\t                f"Cannot load draft model config from \'{speculative_config.model}\'. "\n371\t                f"Please ensure the path is correct and config.json exists. "\n372\t                f"Error: {e}"\n373\t            ) from e\n374\t\n375\t        # ===== Auto-detect draft model class =====\n376\t        draft_neuron_model_cls = None\n377\t        auto_detected_cls = None\n378\t\n379\t        draft_arch = (\n380\t            draft_hf_config_for_inspection.architectures[0]\n381\t            if hasattr(draft_hf_config_for_inspection, "architectures")\n382\t            and draft_hf_config_for_inspection.architectures\n383\t            else None\n384\t        )\n385\t\n386\t        # Check for user-provided draft_neuron_model_class override\n387\t        draft_class_override = None\n388\t        if draft_overrides and "draft_neuron_model_class" in draft_overrides:\n389\t            draft_class_override = draft_overrides.pop("draft_neuron_model_class")\n390\t            logger.info(\n391\t                "User provided draft_neuron_model_class override: \'%s\'",\n392\t                draft_class_override,\n393\t            )\n394\t\n395\t        if draft_arch:\n396\t            logger.info(\n397\t                "Auto-detected draft architecture from config.json: %s", draft_arch\n398\t            )\n399\t            try:\n400\t                auto_detected_cls = _get_neuron_model_cls(draft_arch)\n401\t                logger.info(\n402\t                    "Auto-detected Neuron model class: %s",\n403\t                    auto_detected_cls.__name__,\n404\t                )\n405\t            except ValueError as e:\n406\t                logger.warning(\n407\t                    "Draft architecture \'%s\' is not supported on Neuron. Error: %s",\n408\t                    draft_arch,\n409\t                    e,\n410\t                )\n411\t        else:\n412\t            logger.warning(\n413\t                "No \'architectures\' field found in draft config at %s.",\n414\t                speculative_config.model,\n415\t            )\n416\t\n417\t        # Resolve final draft model class: override > auto-detected > fallback\n418\t        if draft_class_override:\n419\t            try:\n420\t                draft_neuron_model_cls = _get_neuron_model_cls(draft_class_override)\n421\t                if auto_detected_cls:\n422\t                    logger.info(\n423\t                        "Using OVERRIDE class \'%s\' (auto-detected was \'%s\')",\n424\t                        draft_neuron_model_cls.__name__,\n425\t                        auto_detected_cls.__name__,\n426\t                    )\n427\t                else:\n428\t                    logger.info(\n429\t                        "Using OVERRIDE class \'%s\'",\n430\t                        draft_neuron_model_cls.__name__,\n431\t                    )\n432\t            except ValueError as e:\n433\t                logger.warning(\n434\t                    "Override class \'%s\' not found: %s. Falling back.",\n435\t                    draft_class_override,\n436\t                    e,\n437\t                )\n438\t                draft_neuron_model_cls = auto_detected_cls\n439\t        else:\n440\t            draft_neuron_model_cls = auto_detected_cls\n441\t\n442\t        # Fallback to target class if still None\n443\t        if draft_neuron_model_cls is None:\n444\t            draft_neuron_model_cls = neuronx_model_cls\n445\t            logger.info(\n446\t                "Falling back to target model class for draft: %s",\n447\t                draft_neuron_model_cls.__name__,\n448\t            )\n449\t\n450\t        # ===== Create draft config using load_pretrained_config (CALLABLE) =====\n451\t        logger.info(\n452\t            "Creating draft config with class: %s", draft_neuron_model_cls.__name__\n453\t        )\n454\t\n455\t        draft_config = draft_neuron_model_cls.get_config_cls()(\n456\t            draft_neuron_config,\n457\t            load_config=load_pretrained_config(speculative_config.model),\n458\t        )\n459\t\n460\t        # ===== Create and attach fused spec config =====\n461\t        fused_spec_config = FusedSpecNeuronConfig(\n462\t            neuronx_model_cls._model_cls,\n463\t            draft_config=draft_config,\n464\t            draft_model_path=speculative_config.model,\n465\t            draft_model_cls=draft_neuron_model_cls,\n466\t        )\n467\t\n468\t        config.fused_spec_config = fused_spec_config\n469\t        logger.info("Fused speculation config initialized successfully")\n470\t\n471\t\n472\tclass NeuronCausalLM(NeuronModelBase):\n473\t    def _remask_fused_spec_output(self, fused, inputs):\n474\t        """\n475\t        Handle NxDI fused speculation output.\n476\t\n477\t        NxDI fused spec returns:\n478\t        fused[0] = accepted_tokens_with_padding : [B, T], 0-padded\n479\t        fused[-1] = next_pos_ids\n480\t\n481\t        We convert the 0-padding to -1 past the number of tokens actually\n482\t        generated in this step, so the runner can strip pads.\n483\t        """\n484\t        start_time = time.perf_counter()\n485\t\n486\t        accepted_tokens_with_padding = fused[0]\n487\t        next_pos_ids = fused[-1].squeeze(-1)  # [B]\n488\t        positions_vec = inputs["position_ids"][:, -1].to(next_pos_ids.device)\n489\t\n490\t        # Number of tokens generated this step\n491\t        generated_token_counts = (next_pos_ids - positions_vec).to(torch.long)\n492\t\n493\t        # Mask tail with -1 so runner can strip pads\n494\t        B, T = accepted_tokens_with_padding.shape\n495\t        generated_token_counts = generated_token_counts.clamp_(0, T)\n496\t\n497\t        masked = accepted_tokens_with_padding.clone()\n498\t        for b in range(B):\n499\t            masked[b, generated_token_counts[b] :] = -1\n500\t\n501\t        elapsed_ms = (time.perf_counter() - start_time) * 1000\n502\t        logger.debug(\n503\t            "[PERF]     _remask_fused_spec_output: %.2fms [batch=%d]", elapsed_ms, B\n504\t        )\n505\t\n506\t        return masked\n507\t\n508\t    def forward(self, input_ids, input_block_ids, **kwargs):\n509\t        forward_start = time.perf_counter()\n510\t        batch_size = (\n511\t            input_ids.shape[0]\n512\t            if isinstance(input_ids, torch.Tensor)\n513\t            else len(input_ids)\n514\t        )\n515\t\n516\t        with self._reordered(input_block_ids, input_ids=input_ids, **kwargs) as (\n517\t            sorted_ids,\n518\t            inputs,\n519\t            restore,\n520\t        ):\n521\t            # Time model execution\n522\t            model_start = time.perf_counter()\n523\t            output = self.model(\n524\t                inputs["input_ids"],\n525\t                attention_mask=None,\n526\t                seq_ids=sorted_ids,\n527\t                block_table=inputs["block_tables"],\n528\t                **{\n529\t                    k: v\n530\t                    for k, v in inputs.items()\n531\t                    if k\n532\t                    not in ["input_ids", "block_tables", "prefill_completion_state"]\n533\t                },\n534\t            )\n535\t            model_elapsed = (time.perf_counter() - model_start) * 1000\n536\t            logger.debug("[PERF]     model_execution: %.2fms", model_elapsed)\n537\t\n538\t            # Time output processing\n539\t            output_proc_start = time.perf_counter()\n540\t            if self.model.config.neuron_config.on_device_sampling_config:\n541\t                output = output.hidden_states\n542\t                if getattr(\n543\t                    self.model.config.neuron_config, "enable_fused_speculation", False\n544\t                ):\n545\t                    fused = output\n546\t                    output = self._remask_fused_spec_output(fused, inputs)\n547\t            else:\n548\t                if self.neuron_config.is_chunked_prefill:\n549\t                    assert kwargs.get("prefill_completion_state") is not None\n550\t                    idx_for_sampling = (\n551\t                        kwargs["prefill_completion_state"].nonzero().flatten()\n552\t                    )\n553\t                    output = output.logits[0, idx_for_sampling, :]\n554\t                else:\n555\t                    output = output.logits[:, -1, :]\n556\t            output_proc_elapsed = (time.perf_counter() - output_proc_start) * 1000\n557\t            logger.debug("[PERF]     output_processing: %.2fms", output_proc_elapsed)\n558\t\n559\t            # Time restore operation\n560\t            restore_start = time.perf_counter()\n561\t            result = restore(output)\n562\t            restore_elapsed = (time.perf_counter() - restore_start) * 1000\n563\t            logger.debug("[PERF]     restore: %.2fms", restore_elapsed)\n564\t\n565\t            forward_elapsed = (time.perf_counter() - forward_start) * 1000\n566\t            logger.debug(\n567\t                "[PERF]   forward() total: %.2fms [batch=%d]",\n568\t                forward_elapsed,\n569\t                batch_size,\n570\t            )\n571\t\n572\t            return result\n573\t\n574\t    def sample(self, logits: torch.Tensor) -> SamplerOutput | None:\n575\t        if self.model.config.neuron_config.on_device_sampling_config:\n576\t            return SamplerOutput(\n577\t                # The sampled tokens are expanded to 2D tensor with shape\n578\t                # [num_requests, 1], where each row represents one generated\n579\t                # token per request.\n580\t                sampled_token_ids=logits.unsqueeze(-1),\n581\t                logprobs_tensors=None,\n582\t            )\n583\t        else:\n584\t            # CPU sampling is now handled by the model runner\n585\t            # This should not be called when on_device_sampling_config is None\n586\t            # as the model runner will use its own CPU sampler\n587\t            raise RuntimeError(\n588\t                "CPU sampling should be handled by the model runner, not the model. "\n589\t                "This indicates a bug in the sampling path routing."\n590\t            )\n591\t\n592\t    def load_weights(self, model_name_or_path: str, architecture: str, **kwargs):\n593\t        neuronx_model_cls = _get_neuron_model_cls(architecture)\n594\t        success, compiled_model_path, config = self._load_weights_common(\n595\t            model_name_or_path, neuronx_model_cls, **kwargs\n596\t        )\n597\t\n598\t        if not success:\n599\t            if not os.path.exists(model_name_or_path):\n600\t                model_name_or_path = self._save_pretrained_model(model_name_or_path)\n601\t            self._compile_and_load_model(\n602\t                model_name_or_path, neuronx_model_cls, config, compiled_model_path\n603\t            )\n604\t        return success, compiled_model_path\n605\t\n606\t\n607\tclass NeuronMultiModalCausalLM(NeuronCausalLM):\n608\t    def load_weights(self, model_name_or_path: str, architecture: str, **kwargs):\n609\t        neuronx_model_cls = _get_neuron_model_cls(architecture)\n610\t\n611\t        # Neuron ImageToText model configs have nested text and vision config\n612\t        # each has their own neuron_config. The structure looks like:\n613\t        # ImageToTextInferenceConfig\n614\t        # ├── text_config\n615\t        # |   ├── text_neuron_config\n616\t        # |   |   └── ... ...\n617\t        # |   ├── text_config_arg0\n618\t        # |   └── ... ...\n619\t        # ├── vision_config\n620\t        # |   ├── vision_neuron_config\n621\t        # |   |   └── ... ...\n622\t        # |   ├── vision_config_arg0\n623\t        # |   └── ... ...\n624\t        # └── neuron_config (default to same as text_neuron_config)\n625\t        # so we override text and vision neuron_config individually\n626\t\n627\t        default_neuron_config = kwargs["neuron_config"]\n628\t        override_neuron_config = _validate_image_to_text_override_neuron_config(\n629\t            kwargs["override_neuron_config"]\n630\t        )\n631\t\n632\t        vision_neuron_config = copy.deepcopy(default_neuron_config)\n633\t        vision_neuron_config.update(\n634\t            override_neuron_config.get("vision_neuron_config", {})\n635\t        )\n636\t        vision_neuron_config = neuronx_model_cls.get_neuron_config_cls()(\n637\t            **vision_neuron_config\n638\t        )\n639\t\n640\t        text_neuron_config = copy.deepcopy(default_neuron_config)\n641\t        text_neuron_config.update(override_neuron_config.get("text_neuron_config", {}))\n642\t        text_neuron_config = neuronx_model_cls.get_neuron_config_cls()(\n643\t            **text_neuron_config\n644\t        )\n645\t\n646\t        config = neuronx_model_cls.get_config_cls()(\n647\t            text_neuron_config=text_neuron_config,\n648\t            vision_neuron_config=vision_neuron_config,\n649\t            load_config=load_pretrained_config(model_name_or_path),\n650\t        )\n651\t\n652\t        success, compiled_model_path, _ = self._load_weights_common(\n653\t            model_name_or_path, neuronx_model_cls, config=config, **kwargs\n654\t        )\n655\t\n656\t architecture: Either:\n963\t            - HuggingFace architecture (e.g., "LlamaForCausalLM")\n964\t            - Neuron class name (e.g., "NeuronLlamaForCausalLM")\n965\t\n966\t    Returns:\n967\t        Neuron model class\n968\t\n969\t    Examples:\n970\t        _get_neuron_model_cls("LlamaForCausalLM")\n971\t        <class \'NeuronLlamaForCausalLM\'>\n972\t\n973\t _get_default_neuron_config(\n1096\t    model_config: ModelConfig,\n1097\t    cache_config: CacheConfig,\n1098\t    parallel_config: ParallelConfig,\n1099\t    scheduler_config: SchedulerConfig,\n1100\t    lora_serving_config: LoraServingConfig,\n1101\t    speculative_config: SpeculativeConfig | None,\n1102\t):\n1103\t    on_device_sampling_config = }\n1146\t\n1147\t    # Enable fused speculation flags when requested\n1148\t    if speculative_config is not None:\n1149\t        neuron_config["enable_fused_speculation"] = True\n1150\t neuron_config: dict, override_neuron_config: dict\n1160\t) -> dict:\n1161\t    """Handle the pa_num_blocks increment logic to ensure vLLM and NxDI have consistent block counts."""\n1162\t    if cache_config.num_gpu_blocks_override is not None:\n1163\t        pa_num_blocks = neuron_config.get("pa_num_blocks")\n1164\t        original_user_override = (\n1165\t            cache_config.num_gpu_blocks_override - 1\n1166\t        )  # Remove the +1 increment to get original user value\n1167\t\n1168\t        # Check if pa_num_blocks was explicitly set in override_neuron_config\n1169\t        pa_num_blocks_explicitly_set = (\n1170\t            override_neuron_config and "pa_num_blocks" in override_neuron_config\n1171\t        )\n1172\t\n1173\t        if pa_num_blocks_explicitly_set:\n1174\t            # User explicitly set pa_num_blocks, it must match their original intent\n1175\t            if pa_num_blocks == original_user_override:\n1176\t                # User provided original intended value, increment pa_num_blocks to match the incremented num_gpu_blocks_override\n1177\t                neuron_config["pa_num_blocks"] = cache_config.num_gpu_blocks_override\n1178\t                logger.info(\n1179\t                    "User provided pa_num_blocks (%s) matching original --num-gpu-blocks-override intent. "\n1180\t                    "Incrementing pa_num_blocks to %s to match the increment for a null block in vllm.",\n1181\t                    pa_num_blocks,\n1182\t                    cache_config.num_gpu_blocks_override,\n1183\t                )\n1184\t            else:\n1185\t                # pa_num_blocks doesn\'t match the original user intent, this creates a mismatch\n1186\t                raise ValueError(\n1187\t                    f"pa_num_blocks ({pa_num_blocks}) must match your --num-gpu-blocks-override intent({original_user_override}) to ensure vLLM and NxDI have consistent block counts. [{'tool_use_id': 'toolu_bdrk_019VuaRJLnC5uJ4PBpmwdjhW', 'type': 'tool_result', 'content': [{'type': 'text', 'text': 'Now I have a comprehensive understanding of the entire codebase. Let me assemble the implementation plan.\n\n---\n\n## Implementation Plan: Chunked Prefill Support for vllm-neuron\n\n### Executive Summary\n\nChunked prefill has extensive scaffolding already implemented across both vllm_neuron and NxDI. The vllm_neuron model runner has complete input preparation code. NxDI has the bucket generation, KV cache initialization, and configuration plumbing. The single hard blocker is a `NotImplementedError` at NxDI `model_base.py:3054-3055`. However, simply removing that raises exposes three deeper issues that must also be resolved:\n\n1. **Model dispatch in `_get_model_outputs`** -- the method only passes `slot_mapping`/`block_table` to the CTE model in the `is_prefix_caching` branch; the plain `_is_prefill` branch does not, which breaks block KV writes\n2. **Hidden state slicing** -- at `NeuronBaseModel.forward()` line 964-976, the model extracts only a single hidden state (at `max(position_ids)`), discarding the full-sequence logits that chunked prefill needs\n3. **Input generator for compilation** -- `ModelWrapper.input_generator()` has no chunked prefill branch, so the model cannot be traced with the correct input signature (including `slot_mapping`, `block_table`, etc.)\n\nSince NxDI is a preinstalled package and cannot be recompiled, all fixes must be applied as monkey-patches from the vllm_neuron layer.\n\n---\n\n### Phase 1: Bypass the NotImplementedError\n\n**Approach**: Monkey-patch `NeuronBaseForCausalLM.__init__` before model instantiation.\n\n**Where to patch**: In `vllm_neuron/worker/neuronx_distributed_model_loader.py`, inside `_load_weights_common` (around line 187), BEFORE the model class is instantiated.\n\n**Implementation**:\n```python\n# At the top of _load_weights_common or in a helper function\nfrom neuronx_distributed_inference.models.model_base import NeuronBaseForCausalLM\n\n_original_nxdi_init = NeuronBaseForCausalLM.__init__\n\ndef _patched_nxdi_init(self, *args, **kwargs):\n    # Temporarily disable the NotImplementedError guard\n    # Save the is_chunked_prefill state, set to False, call init, restore\n    # OR: patch with a version that skips the check and continues to enable_context_encoding/enable_token_generation\n    _original_nxdi_init(self, *args, **kwargs)\n\n# The cleaner approach: patch only the specific check\n```\n\nA cleaner pattern is to subclass. Since the vllm_neuron layer already instantiates models through `neuronx_model_cls(...)`, we can create a wrapper that intercepts initialization. However, the simplest reliable approach is:\n\n**Strategy A (Preferred)**: Before calling the NxDI model constructor, monkey-patch `NeuronBaseForCausalLM.__init__` to replace the `NotImplementedError` block with the proper initialization logic:\n\n```python\ndef _chunked_prefill_init_patch(original_init):\n    def patched_init(self, *args, **kwargs):\n        # Store the flag before original init\n        # The original init raises if is_chunked_prefill is True\n        # We need to bypass that and instead do what the code AFTER the raise does\n        \n        # Option: temporarily patch neuron_config.is_chunked_prefill = False,\n        # call original_init, then restore and call enable_context_encoding + enable_token_generation manually\n        ...\n    return patched_init\n```\n\n**Strategy B (More surgical)**: Since the `NotImplementedError` occurs between `self.model_wrapper = self.get_model_wrapper_cls()` (line 3052) and `self.enable_context_encoding()` (line 3062), we can:\n1. Temporarily set `neuron_config.is_chunked_prefill = False` in the config\n2. Call the original init (which will skip the check and proceed normally to `enable_context_encoding` + `enable_token_generation`)\n3. After init, restore `neuron_config.is_chunked_prefill = True`\n\nBut this is incorrect because `enable_context_encoding` needs `is_chunked_prefill=True` to generate the correct 2D buckets via `generate_buckets_for_cte` -> `generate_buckets_for_chunked_prefill_cte`.\n\n**Strategy C (Best)**: Patch `NeuronBaseForCausalLM.__init__` to skip ONLY the `NotImplementedError` raise. Replace the method such that lines 3054-3055 are simply omitted. The rest of `__init__` already does the right thing: it calls `enable_context_encoding()` and then `enable_token_generation()` (or skips TKG if `tkg_model_enabled=False` in ChunkedPrefillConfig).\n\nWait -- examining line 3057-3068, after the `NotImplementedError` would have been raised, the code continues with:\n```python\nif self.neuron_config.enable_fused_speculation:\n    ...\nelse:\n    self.enable_context_encoding()\n    if self.neuron_config.speculation_length > 0:\n        self.enable_speculation()\n    elif ...:\n        ...\n    else:\n        self.enable_token_generation()\n```\n\nFor chunked prefill:\n- CTE model: `enable_context_encoding()` will set `n_active_tokens = max_context_length` (= chunk_size) and call `generate_buckets_for_cte()` which dispatches to `generate_buckets_for_chunked_prefill_cte()`\n- TKG model: `enable_token_generation()` will create the separate decode model (only if `tkg_model_enabled=True` in ChunkedPrefillConfig)\n\nThe correct patch is to JUST skip the raise. If we use the `tkg_model_enabled=False` path, only the CTE model is compiled (all requests including decodes go through CTE).\n\n---\n\n### Phase 2: Fix Model Dispatch in `_get_model_outputs`\n\n**Problem**: When `is_prefix_caching=False` and `is_chunked_prefill=True`, the method enters `elif self._is_prefill(position_ids):` at line 3632, which calls `context_encoding_model(input_ids, attention_mask, position_ids, seq_ids, sampling_params, prev_hidden, adapter_ids, *llava_args)` -- WITHOUT passing `slot_mapping`, `block_table`, `full_context_lens`, or `computed_context_lens`.\n\n**Why this matters**: The block KV cache manager\'s `update_cache` method needs `slot_mapping` to write new KV entries. The `get_cache` method needs `active_block_table` to read KV entries. Without these, the model will fail during attention computation.\n\n**Solution**: Monkey-patch `NeuronBaseForCausalLM._get_model_outputs` to add a chunked prefill dispatch branch BEFORE the `elif self._is_prefill(position_ids)` check.\n\nThe chunked prefill dispatch should:\n1. Always route to `context_encoding_model` (since batch_size=1, all inputs are concatenated into one "mega-sequence")\n2. Pass `slot_mapping`, `block_table` (as `active_block_table`), `full_context_lens`, and `computed_context_lens`\n3. Compute `num_queries = full_context_lens - computed_context_lens`\n\nThe input signature for the CTE model with block KV follows the `is_prefix_caching` pattern:\n```python\noutputs = self.context_encoding_model(\n    input_ids,\n    attention_mask,\n    position_ids,\n    seq_ids,\n    sampling_params,\n    torch.empty(0),  # prev_hidden\n    adapter_ids,\n    torch.empty(0), torch.empty(0), torch.empty(0), torch.empty(0),  # placeholders\n    slot_mapping,\n    block_table,\n    num_queries,\n    computed_context_lens,\n)\n```\n\nHowever, this input signature must EXACTLY match what the compiled model expects. Since we cannot recompile, the input_generator must also be patched for chunked prefill (Phase 5).\n\n**Alternative approach**: Since `is_prefix_caching` and `is_chunked_prefill` share the same block KV infrastructure, set BOTH `is_prefix_caching=True` AND `is_chunked_prefill=True` in the config. This leverages the existing `is_prefix_caching` dispatch path which already passes `slot_mapping` and `block_table`. The `BlockKVCacheManager` already handles the distinction: when `is_chunked_prefill=True`, it uses `_get_cache_for_chunked_prefill` which returns the raw cache for CTE and does block-table selection for TKG.\n\nBUT: the config validation at line 308-311 asserts:\n```python\nassert self.is_block_kv_layout, "is_block_kv_layout has to be true for chunked prefill"\n```\nAnd `CHUNKED_ATTENTION_SUPPORTED_NEURON_CONFIG` at line 28 has `is_prefix_caching: False` combined with `is_chunked_prefill: False`, meaning the "chunked attention" (a different feature -- fixed-size attention window for long contexts) does not support either. This is separate from "chunked prefill."\n\nThe conclusion: we CANNOT just set `is_prefix_caching=True` because that triggers a different code path in the KV cache manager (`_get_block_cache_and_reshape_bhsd` instead of `_get_cache_for_chunked_prefill`). We need the monkey-patch approach.\n\n---\n\n### Phase 3: Fix Hidden State / Logit Extraction\n\n**Problem**: At `NeuronBaseModel.forward()` line 964-976, after `get_model_output` returns, the code does:\n```python\nif not self.sliced_hidden:\n    index = torch.max(position_ids, dim=1, keepdim=True).indices\n    hidden_states = torch.gather(hidden_states, dim=1, index=...)\n```\n\nThis extracts only the SINGLE token at max position. For chunked prefill (batch_size=1), we need hidden states for ALL positions because the vllm_neuron layer extracts specific indices via `prefill_completion_state`.\n\n**Solution options**:\n\nOption A: Set `output_logits=True` in the NeuronConfig. When `output_logits=True`, the model returns BOTH the sampled/extracted result AND the full logits tensor (see line 1018-1024). The vllm_neuron layer uses `output.logits[0, idx_for_sampling, :]` to extract per-request logits.\n\nBUT: the slicing STILL happens (it happens before `lm_head` and logit computation). The `output_logits` flag causes the full logits to be appended to outputs as a second element, but those logits are computed AFTER `hidden_states` is sliced. So this does not help.\n\nOption B: Disable on-device sampling for chunked prefill AND skip the hidden-state slicing. For chunked prefill, the model should NOT slice hidden_states at all. Instead, it should run lm_head on the full sequence and return all logits. The vllm_neuron layer then selects the appropriate logit positions.\n\nThe hidden_states slicing at line 964-976 occurs inside `NeuronBaseModel.forward()`. For chunked prefill:\n- `self.sliced_hidden` is False (since sequence_parallel is typically disabled for CTE in chunked prefill with batch_size=1)\n- `position_ids.shape[-1]` is the chunk_size (not 1 and not speculation_length)\n- So it WILL enter the slicing branch\n\n**The fix**: Monkey-patch `NeuronBaseModel.forward()` to skip the slicing when `is_chunked_prefill=True`. OR: more precisely, the issue is that `self._is_context_encoding(input_ids)` returns True for chunked prefill, and the slicing code runs for CTE. We need to either:\n\n1. Make the model NOT slice for chunked prefill, OR\n2. Make the model return full logits for chunked prefill\n\nThe most elegant approach: When `is_chunked_prefill=True`, skip the hidden_state gathering entirely. The `lm_head` runs on `hidden_states` of shape `[1, chunk_size, hidden_dim]` and produces logits of shape `[1, chunk_size, vocab_size]`. The vllm_neuron layer then extracts `logits[0, idx_for_sampling, :]`.\n\n**BUT**: This has compilation implications. The model is traced with a specific output shape. If we skip the slicing, the output shape changes from `[1, 1, vocab_size]` to `[1, chunk_size, vocab_size]`. This means the compiled model must know at trace time that slicing is skipped.\n\nThis is where the monkey-patching gets complex. Since the model is traced/compiled during `enable_context_encoding()`, the forward method behavior at trace time determines the compiled NEFF. We need to ensure the model is compiled without the slicing.\n\n**Key insight**: The chunked prefill CTE model MUST be compiled with the full-sequence output (no last-token extraction). This means we need to patch `NeuronBaseModel.forward()` BEFORE compilation happens. Since compilation happens inside `NeuronBaseForCausalLM.__init__` -> `enable_context_encoding()` -> `model_wrapper.trace()`, we need the patch applied early.\n\n---\n\n### Phase 4: Disable On-Device Sampling for Chunked Prefill CTE\n\n**Problem**: The default config creates `OnDeviceSamplingConfig(dynamic=True, deterministic=False)`. With on-device sampling, the model internally samples tokens and returns them. For chunked prefill, we need raw logits for ALL positions (not just sampled tokens at a single position).\n\n**Solution**: Set `on_device_sampling_config=None` in the neuron config when `enable_chunked_prefill=True`. This is partially addressed already in `_get_default_neuron_config` (the code already sets `batch_size=1` and `max_context_length=max_num_batched_tokens` for chunked prefill). But `on_device_sampling_config` is ALWAYS set.\n\n**Implementation**: In `_get_default_neuron_config`, add:\n```python\nif scheduler_config.enable_chunked_prefill:\n    on_device_sampling_config = None  # Need full logits for all positions\n```\n\nOr alternatively, disable it via the `NEURON_ON_DEVICE_SAMPLING_DISABLED=1` environment variable.\n\n---\n\n### Phase 5: Handle Model Compilation (Input Generator)\n\n**Problem**: `ModelWrapper.input_generator()` does not have a chunked prefill branch. The compiled model needs to accept `slot_mapping`, `block_table`, `num_queries`, `computed_context_lens` as inputs (matching the dispatch call signature).\n\n**Solution**: Monkey-patch `ModelWrapper.input_generator` to handle the chunked prefill case, generating trace inputs that include:\n- `input_ids`: shape `[1, chunk_size]` (batch_size=1)\n- `attention_mask`: shape `[1, chunk_size]`\n- `position_ids`: shape `[1, chunk_size]`\n- `seq_ids`: shape `[1]`\n- `sampling_params`: appropriate shape\n- `prev_hidden`: `torch.empty(0)`\n- `adapter_ids`: shape `[1]`\n- `slot_mapping`: shape `[1, chunk_size]` (for block KV writes)\n- `block_table`: shape `[max_num_seqs, max_blocks_per_seq]` (for KV reads)\n- `num_queries`: shape `[max_num_seqs, 1]` (how many new tokens per request)\n- `computed_context_lens`: shape `[max_num_seqs, 1]` (previously computed context)\n\nThe `input_generator` must produce inputs for EACH bucket. The 2D buckets are `[chunk_size, num_tiles]` pairs from `generate_buckets_for_chunked_prefill_cte`.\n\n---\n\n### Phase 6: Scheduler Configuration\n\n**Approach**: Use `DISABLE_NEURON_CUSTOM_SCHEDULER=1` to enable the vLLM V1 native scheduler with chunked prefill.\n\nThe platform.py code at line 381 already handles this:\n```python\nif disable_scheduler_override:\n    # The vLLM V1 native scheduler will be used with chunked prefill enabled.\n    assert vllm_config.cache_config.block_size is not None\n```\n\nThe native V1 scheduler has built-in chunked prefill support and will produce `SchedulerOutput` with `num_scheduled_tokens` per request, mixed prefill+decode batches, etc. The model runner\'s `_prepare_chunked_prefill_inputs` already handles this scheduler output format.\n\n---\n\n### Phase 7: The `is_context_encoding` Detection Problem\n\n**Analysis**: In `NeuronBaseForCausalLM.forward()` at line 3348:\n```python\nis_context_encoding = input_ids.shape[-1] > 1 and not position_ids.min().item()\n```\n\nFor chunked prefill with batch_size=1:\n- `input_ids.shape[-1]` = chunk_size (always > 1)\n- `position_ids.min()` = the minimum position in the concatenated chunk\n\nThe second condition `not position_ids.min().item()` means `position_ids.min() == 0`. In chunked prefill, the chunk always contains at least one request whose first token is at position 0 (a new prefill starting), OR it may contain only decode tokens (where all positions > 0).\n\nWhen the chunk contains ONLY decode tokens (all `position_ids > 0`), `is_context_encoding` will be False. This would incorrectly route to the TKG model. But with chunked prefill (no separate TKG model, `tkg_model_enabled=False`), there IS no TKG model.\n\n**Solution**: When `is_chunked_prefill=True`:\n- Always route to `context_encoding_model` regardless of `is_context_encoding`\n- The CTE model handles both prefill and decode tokens in the same forward pass\n\nThe monkey-patch for `_get_model_outputs` (Phase 2) should handle this by checking `self.neuron_config.is_chunked_prefill` FIRST, before the `is_prefix_caching` or `_is_prefill` checks.\n\n---\n\n### Phase 8: Configuration Requirements\n\nWhen launching with chunked prefill:\n\n```bash\nDISABLE_NEURON_CUSTOM_SCHEDULER=1 \\\nNEURON_ON_DEVICE_SAMPLING_DISABLED=1 \\\npython -m vllm.entrypoints.openai.api_server \\\n    --model <model_path> \\\n    --device neuron \\\n    --override-neuron-config \'{"chunked_prefill_config": {"max_num_seqs": 8, "tkg_model_enabled": false, "kernel_q_tile_size": 128, "kernel_kv_tile_size": 1024}}\' \\\n    --block-size 128 \\\n    --max-num-batched-tokens 2048 \\\n    --max-num-seqs 8 \\\n    --num-gpu-blocks-override <calculated>\n```\n\n---\n\n### Implementation Order\n\n1. **Create a chunked prefill patch module**: `/path/to/vllm_neuron/worker/chunked_prefill_patches.py`\n2. **Monkey-patch NeuronBaseForCausalLM.__init__**: Skip NotImplementedError\n3. **Monkey-patch NeuronBaseModel.forward()**: Skip hidden-state slicing for chunked prefill\n4. **Monkey-patch NeuronBaseForCausalLM._get_model_outputs**: Add chunked prefill dispatch branch\n5. **Monkey-patch ModelWrapper.input_generator**: Add chunked prefill input shapes\n6. **Modify `_get_default_neuron_config`**: Disable on-device sampling for chunked prefill\n7. **Apply patches in model loader**: Before model instantiation in `NeuronCausalLM._load_weights_common`\n8. **Testing**: Unit tests for input preparation, integration test with small model\n\n---\n\n### Risks and Mitigations\n\n| Risk | Impact | Mitigation |\n|------|--------|------------|\n| Attention kernel does not support chunked prefill tile patterns | Model compilation fails | The bucket generation code exists and is tested; NKI kernels for block KV are already in place |\n| Full-sequence lm_head causes memory pressure | OOM on large chunk sizes | Limit chunk_size via `max_num_batched_tokens`; use smaller buckets |\n| Monkey-patches break on NxDI version upgrades | Runtime errors | Version-pin NxDI; add defensive checks for method signatures |\n| 2D bucketing creates too many compilation targets | Long compilation time | Limit bucket count in `generate_buckets_on_chunk_size` |\n| Mixed decode+prefill attention mask is incorrect | Wrong outputs | The existing `create_attn_mask` for CTE produces a causal mask along the full concatenated sequence; verify correctness |\n\n---\n\n### Critical Files for Implementation\n- `/opt/aws_neuronx_venv_pytorch_inference_vllm_0_16/lib/python3.12/site-packages/vllm_neuron/worker/neuronx_distributed_model_loader.py` -- where monkey-patches must be applied before model instantiation, and where `_get_default_neuron_config` disables on-device sampling for chunked prefill\n- `/opt/aws_neuronx_venv_pytorch_inference_vllm_0_16/lib/python3.12/site-packages/neuronx_distributed_inference/models/model_base.py` -- contains the three methods to monkey-patch: `NeuronBaseForCausalLM.__init__` (line 3054), `NeuronBaseModel.forward` (line 964-976), and `NeuronBaseForCausalLM._get_model_outputs` (line 3549)\n- `/opt/aws_neuronx_venv_pytorch_inference_vllm_0_16/lib/python3.12/site-packages/neuronx_distributed_inference/models/model_wrapper.py` -- `ModelWrapper.input_generator` (line 206) needs a chunked prefill trace-input branch\n- `/opt/aws_neuronx_venv_pytorch_inference_vllm_0_16/lib/python3.12/site-packages/vllm_neuron/worker/neuronx_distributed_model_runner.py` -- already complete chunked prefill input preparation; only minor adjustments needed for on-device-sampling disabled path\n- `/opt/aws_neuronx_venv_pytorch_inference_vllm_0_16/lib/python3.12/site-packages/vllm_neuron/platform.py` -- scheduling configuration (line 349-397); already handles `DISABLE_NEURON_CUSTOM_SCHEDULER`'}]}]

## ASSISTANT (2026-07-20 10:43:07)

[{'type': 'tool_use', 'id': 'toolu_bdrk_01Uetiz7RfncLYbHYWudRDS8', 'name': 'Write', 'input': {'file_path': '/dev3/cc/plans/https-github-com-vllm-project-vllm-neuro-polished-starfish.md', 'content': '# Chunked Prefill for vllm-neuron: Implementation Plan\n\n## Context\n\nNeuron vllm (`vllm_neuron` plugin + NxDI library) currently does not support chunked prefill. However, **most of the code paths already exist** -- both the vllm_neuron model runner (input preparation, logit extraction) and NxDI (bucket generation, block KV cache, config) have full scaffolding in place. The single hard blocker is a `raise NotImplementedError` in NxDI `model_base.py:3054-3055`, placed there because the NxDI forward pass and model compilation were never finalized for this feature.\n\nSince NxDI is a preinstalled package (`neuronx_distributed_inference`), all fixes must be applied as **monkey-patches from the vllm_neuron layer** before model instantiation.\n\n## What Chunked Prefill Gives Us\n\n- **Reduced TTFT for short requests**: decode requests no longer starved behind long prefills\n- **Better hardware utilization**: mix prefill chunks + decode tokens in one forward pass\n- **Bounded latency**: chunk size = `max_num_batched_tokens` caps the compute per step\n\n---\n\n## Architecture (Already in Place)\n\n```\nScheduler (vLLM V1 native, chunked prefill enabled)\n    |\n    v\nSchedulerOutput (num_scheduled_tokens per request)\n    |\n    v\nNeuronxDistributedModelRunner._prepare_chunked_prefill_inputs()\n    - Concatenates all scheduled tokens into one mega-sequence (batch_size=1)\n    - Computes slot_mapping, block_tables, position_ids, prefill_completion_state\n    |\n    v\nNeuronCausalLM.forward()\n    - Routes to NxDI model_base.NeuronBaseForCausalLM.forward()\n    - Dispatches to CTE model (always, for chunked prefill)\n    - CTE runs attention on [1, chunk_size] input using block KV cache\n    - Returns logits [1, chunk_size, vocab_size]\n    |\n    v\nvllm_neuron extracts per-request logits using prefill_completion_state\n    - Incomplete prefills: logits masked to -inf\n    - Complete prefills + decode: feed to sampler\n```\n\n---\n\n## Implementation Steps\n\n### Step 1: Bypass the NotImplementedError\n\n**File**: `neuronx_distributed_inference/models/model_base.py` line 3054  \n**Method**: Monkey-patch `NeuronBaseForCausalLM.__init__`\n\nThe raise occurs between `self.model_wrapper = self.get_model_wrapper_cls()` (line 3052) and the `enable_context_encoding()` call (line 3062). After the raise is skipped, the existing code proceeds correctly:\n- `enable_context_encoding()` creates CTE with 2D buckets via `generate_buckets_for_chunked_prefill_cte()`\n- `enable_token_generation()` creates TKG (if `tkg_model_enabled=True` in ChunkedPrefillConfig)\n\n**Patch approach**: Wrap the original `__init__` and catch + suppress only the specific `NotImplementedError` with the known message string, then let execution continue past it.\n\n### Step 2: Fix Model Dispatch (`_get_model_outputs`)\n\n**File**: `neuronx_distributed_inference/models/model_base.py` line 3549  \n**Problem**: When `is_chunked_prefill=True` but `is_prefix_caching=False`, the code falls through to the `elif self._is_prefill(position_ids):` branch which does NOT pass `slot_mapping` / `block_table` to the CTE model. Without these, the block KV cache manager cannot read/write correctly.\n\n**Also**: The `is_context_encoding` detection (`input_ids.shape[-1] > 1 and position_ids.min() == 0`) can misroute decode-only chunks to TKG (which may not exist).\n\n**Fix**: Add a `is_chunked_prefill` dispatch branch at the TOP of `_get_model_outputs`, before the `is_prefix_caching` check. This branch:\n1. Always routes to `context_encoding_model`\n2. Passes `slot_mapping`, `block_table`, `full_context_lens`, `computed_context_lens`\n3. Computes `num_queries = full_context_lens - computed_context_lens`\n\n### Step 3: Fix Hidden State Slicing in NeuronBaseModel.forward()\n\n**File**: `neuronx_distributed_inference/models/model_base.py` ~line 964  \n**Problem**: After the model runs, the code extracts ONLY the last-position hidden state:\n```python\nindex = torch.max(position_ids, dim=1, keepdim=True).indices\nhidden_states = torch.gather(hidden_states, dim=1, index=...)\n```\n\nFor chunked prefill, we need the FULL sequence of logits (shape `[1, chunk_size, vocab_size]`) because the vllm_neuron layer extracts specific indices via `prefill_completion_state.nonzero()`.\n\n**Fix**: Monkey-patch `NeuronBaseModel.forward()` to skip hidden-state slicing when `is_chunked_prefill=True`. This also affects compilation -- the traced model must produce full-sequence output.\n\n**Compilation implication**: The compiled CTE model for chunked prefill must be traced WITHOUT the slicing. This means the patch must be applied BEFORE `enable_context_encoding()` triggers model tracing.\n\n### Step 4: Disable On-Device Sampling for Chunked Prefill\n\n**File**: `vllm_neuron/worker/neuronx_distributed_model_loader.py` `_get_default_neuron_config()`  \n**Problem**: On-device sampling extracts a single sampled token per position. Chunked prefill needs raw logits for all positions so the vllm_neuron layer can select and mask appropriately.\n\n**Fix**: When `scheduler_config.enable_chunked_prefill`:\n```python\non_device_sampling_config = None\n```\n\nThe CPU sampling path in the model runner already handles this case correctly (the model runner has `_prepare_logits_for_sampling` + `cpu_sampler`).\n\n### Step 5: Input Generator for Compilation\n\n**File**: `neuronx_distributed_inference/models/model_wrapper.py` `input_generator()` ~line 206  \n**Problem**: The input generator creates trace inputs for model compilation. It has no chunked prefill branch, so the model would be traced without `slot_mapping`/`block_table` inputs.\n\n**Fix**: Monkey-patch `input_generator` to produce the correct signature when `is_chunked_prefill=True`:\n- `input_ids`: `[1, bucket_chunk_size]`\n- `attention_mask`: `[1, bucket_chunk_size]`\n- `position_ids`: `[1, bucket_chunk_size]`\n- `seq_ids`: `[1]`\n- `sampling_params`: standard\n- `slot_mapping`: `[1, bucket_chunk_size]`\n- `block_table`: `[max_num_seqs, max_blocks_per_seq]`\n- `full_context_lens`: `[max_num_seqs]`\n- `computed_context_lens`: `[max_num_seqs]`\n\n### Step 6: Scheduler Configuration\n\n**Already supported**: Set `DISABLE_NEURON_CUSTOM_SCHEDULER=1` to use vLLM V1 native scheduler with built-in chunked prefill logic.\n\nThe native scheduler:\n- Splits long prefills into chunks of `max_num_batched_tokens`\n- Mixes prefill chunks + decode tokens in each step\n- Tracks partial prefill state via `num_computed_tokens`\n- Produces `SchedulerOutput.num_scheduled_tokens` per request\n\n### Step 7: Apply All Patches Before Model Load\n\n**File**: `vllm_neuron/worker/neuronx_distributed_model_loader.py`  \n**Where**: Inside `NeuronCausalLM._load_weights_common()`, before `neuronx_model_cls(...)` is called.\n\nAll monkey-patches must be applied in the correct order:\n1. Patch `NeuronBaseModel.forward()` (hidden state slicing)\n2. Patch `ModelWrapper.input_generator()` (compilation inputs)\n3. Patch `NeuronBaseForCausalLM._get_model_outputs()` (dispatch)\n4. Patch `NeuronBaseForCausalLM.__init__()` (skip NotImplementedError)\n\n---\n\n## Files to Modify\n\n| File | Change |\n|------|--------|\n| `vllm_neuron/worker/neuronx_distributed_model_loader.py` | Add monkey-patch application before model load; disable on-device sampling for chunked prefill in `_get_default_neuron_config` |\n| New: `vllm_neuron/worker/chunked_prefill_patches.py` | All monkey-patch functions in one module |\n| `vllm_neuron/platform.py` | Minor: ensure `block_size` assertion is clear for chunked prefill path |\n\n**No changes needed** (already correct):\n- `vllm_neuron/worker/neuronx_distributed_model_runner.py` -- full chunked prefill input preparation already implemented\n- `vllm_neuron/core/scheduler.py` -- bypassed via `max_num_batched_tokens`: Becomes the chunk size (max tokens processed per step)\n- `max_num_seqs`: How many requests can be in-flight (affects KV cache allocation)\n- `tkg_model_enabled: false`: tracing | Apply patch before `enable_context_encoding()` so trace captures correct graph |\n| Monkey-patches fragile across NxDI versions | Gate patches behind version checks; document exact method signatures |\n| Causal mask incorrect for concatenated multi-request chunk | NxDI\'s `_infer_attention_mask` uses position_ids to generate mask; verify it produces per-request causal masks (not global causal) |\n| OOM with large chunk sizes | Start with small `max_num_batched_tokens` (e.g., 1024); scale up after validation |\n\n---\n\n## Alternative Approach: Fork NxDI\n\nIf monkey-patching proves too fragile, the alternative is to fork NxDI and apply changes directly:\n1. [{'tool_use_id': 'toolu_bdrk_011gED2JDN3CrD4zGr8zE46X', 'type': 'tool_result', 'content': '1\t# Chunked Prefill for vllm-neuron: Implementation Plan\n2\t\n3\t## Context\n4\t\n5\tNeuron vllm (`vllm_neuron` plugin + NxDI library) currently does not support chunked prefill. However, **most of the code paths already exist** -- both the vllm_neuron model runner (input preparation, logit extraction) and NxDI (bucket generation, block KV cache, config) have full scaffolding in place. The single hard blocker is a `raise NotImplementedError` in NxDI `model_base.py:3054-3055`, placed there because the NxDI forward pass and model compilation were never finalized for this feature.\n6\t\n7\tSince NxDI is a preinstalled package (`neuronx_distributed_inference`), all fixes must be applied as **monkey-patches from the vllm_neuron layer** before model instantiation.\n8\t\n9\t## What Chunked Prefill Gives Us\n10\t\n11\t- **Reduced TTFT for short requests**: decode requests no longer starved behind long prefills\n12\t- **Better hardware utilization**: mix prefill chunks + decode tokens in one forward pass\n13\t- **Bounded latency**: chunk size = `max_num_batched_tokens` caps the compute per step\n14\t\n15\t---\n16\t\n17\t## Architecture (Already in Place)\n18\t\n19\t```\n20\tScheduler (vLLM V1 native, chunked prefill enabled)\n21\t    |\n22\t    v\n23\tSchedulerOutput (num_scheduled_tokens per request)\n24\t    |\n25\t    v\n26\tNeuronxDistributedModelRunner._prepare_chunked_prefill_inputs()\n27\t    - Concatenates all scheduled tokens into one mega-sequence (batch_size=1)\n28\t    - Computes slot_mapping, block_tables, position_ids, prefill_completion_state\n29\t    |\n30\t    v\n31\tNeuronCausalLM.forward()\n32\t    - Routes to NxDI model_base.NeuronBaseForCausalLM.forward()\n33\t    - Dispatches to CTE model (always, for chunked prefill)\n34\t    - CTE runs attention on [1, chunk_size] input using block KV cache\n35\t    - Returns logits [1, chunk_size, vocab_size]\n36\t    |\n37\t    v\n38\tvllm_neuron extracts per-request logits using prefill_completion_state\n39\t    - Incomplete prefills: logits masked to -inf\n40\t    - Complete prefills + decode: feed to sampler\n41\t```\n42\t\n43\t---\n44\t\n45\t## Implementation Steps\n46\t\n47\t### Step 1: Bypass the NotImplementedError\n48\t\n49\t**File**: `neuronx_distributed_inference/models/model_base.py` line 3054  \n50\t**Method**: Monkey-patch `NeuronBaseForCausalLM.__init__`\n51\t\n52\tThe raise occurs between `self.model_wrapper = self.get_model_wrapper_cls()` (line 3052) and the `enable_context_encoding()` call (line 3062). After the raise is skipped, the existing code proceeds correctly:\n53\t- `enable_context_encoding()` creates CTE with 2D buckets via `generate_buckets_for_chunked_prefill_cte()`\n54\t- `enable_token_generation()` creates TKG (if `tkg_model_enabled=True` in ChunkedPrefillConfig)\n55\t\n56\t**Patch approach**: Wrap the original `__init__` and catch + suppress only the specific `NotImplementedError` with the known message string, then let execution continue past it.\n57\t\n58\t### Step 2: Fix Model Dispatch (`_get_model_outputs`)\n59\t\n60\t**File**: `neuronx_distributed_inference/models/model_base.py` line 3549  \n61\t**Problem**: When `is_chunked_prefill=True` but `is_prefix_caching=False`, the code falls through to the `elif self._is_prefill(position_ids):` branch which does NOT pass `slot_mapping` / `block_table` to the CTE model. Without these, the block KV cache manager cannot read/write correctly.\n62\t\n63\t**Also**: The `is_context_encoding` detection (`input_ids.shape[-1] > 1 and position_ids.min() == 0`) can misroute decode-only chunks to TKG (which may not exist).\n64\t\n65\t**Fix**: Add a `is_chunked_prefill` dispatch branch at the TOP of `_get_model_outputs`, before the `is_prefix_caching` check. This branch:\n66\t1. Always routes to `context_encoding_model`\n67\t2. Passes `slot_mapping`, `block_table`, `full_context_lens`, `computed_context_lens`\n68\t3. Computes `num_queries = full_context_lens - computed_context_lens`\n69\t\n70\t### Step 3: Fix Hidden State Slicing in NeuronBaseModel.forward()\n71\t\n72\t**File**: `neuronx_distributed_inference/models/model_base.py` ~line 964  \n73\t**Problem**: After the model runs, the code extracts ONLY the last-position hidden state:\n74\t```python\n75\tindex = torch.max(position_ids, dim=1, keepdim=True).indices\n76\thidden_states = torch.gather(hidden_states, dim=1, index=...)\n77\t```\n78\t\n79\tFor chunked prefill, we need the FULL sequence of logits (shape `[1, chunk_size, vocab_size]`) because the vllm_neuron layer extracts specific indices via `prefill_completion_state.nonzero()`.\n80\t\n81\t**Fix**: Monkey-patch `NeuronBaseModel.forward()` to skip hidden-state slicing when `is_chunked_prefill=True`. This also affects compilation -- the traced model must produce full-sequence output.\n82\t\n83\t**Compilation implication**: The compiled CTE model for chunked prefill must be traced WITHOUT the slicing. This means the patch must be applied BEFORE `enable_context_encoding()` triggers model tracing.\n84\t\n85\t### Step 4: Disable On-Device Sampling for Chunked Prefill\n86\t\n87\t**File**: `vllm_neuron/worker/neuronx_distributed_model_loader.py` `_get_default_neuron_config()`  \n88\t**Problem**: On-device sampling extracts a single sampled token per position. Chunked prefill needs raw logits for all positions so the vllm_neuron layer can select and mask appropriately.\n89\t\n90\t**Fix**: When `scheduler_config.enable_chunked_prefill`:\n91\t```python\n92\ton_device_sampling_config = None\n93\t```\n94\t\n95\tThe CPU sampling path in the model runner already handles this case correctly (the model runner has `_prepare_logits_for_sampling` + `cpu_sampler`).\n96\t\n97\t### Step 5: Input Generator for Compilation\n98\t\n99\t**File**: `neuronx_distributed_inference/models/model_wrapper.py` `input_generator()` ~line 206  \n100\t**Problem**: The input generator creates trace inputs for model compilation. It has no chunked prefill branch, so the model would be traced without `slot_mapping`/`block_table` inputs.\n101\t\n102\t**Fix**: Monkey-patch `input_generator` to produce the correct signature when `is_chunked_prefill=True`:\n103\t- `input_ids`: `[1, bucket_chunk_size]`\n104\t- `attention_mask`: `[1, bucket_chunk_size]`\n105\t- `position_ids`: `[1, bucket_chunk_size]`\n106\t- `seq_ids`: `[1]`\n107\t- `sampling_params`: standard\n108\t- `slot_mapping`: `[1, bucket_chunk_size]`\n109\t- `block_table`: `[max_num_seqs, max_blocks_per_seq]`\n110\t- `full_context_lens`: `[max_num_seqs]`\n111\t- `computed_context_lens`: `[max_num_seqs]`\n112\t\n113\t### Step 6: Scheduler Configuration\n114\t\n115\t**Already supported**: Set `DISABLE_NEURON_CUSTOM_SCHEDULER=1` to use vLLM V1 native scheduler with built-in chunked prefill logic.\n116\t\n117\tThe native scheduler:\n118\t- Splits long prefills into chunks of `max_num_batched_tokens`\n119\t- Mixes prefill chunks + decode tokens in each step\n120\t- Tracks partial prefill state via `num_computed_tokens`\n121\t- Produces `SchedulerOutput.num_scheduled_tokens` per request\n122\t\n123\t### Step 7: Apply All Patches Before Model Load\n124\t\n125\t**File**: `vllm_neuron/worker/neuronx_distributed_model_loader.py`  \n126\t**Where**: Inside `NeuronCausalLM._load_weights_common()`, before `neuronx_model_cls(...)` is called.\n127\t\n128\tAll monkey-patches must be applied in the correct order:\n129\t1. Patch `NeuronBaseModel.forward()` (hidden state slicing)\n130\t2. Patch `ModelWrapper.input_generator()` (compilation inputs)\n131\t3. Patch `NeuronBaseForCausalLM._get_model_outputs()` (dispatch)\n132\t4. Patch `NeuronBaseForCausalLM.__init__()` (skip NotImplementedError)\n133\t\n134\t---\n135\t\n136\t## Files to Modify\n137\t\n138\t| File | Change |\n139\t|------|--------|\n140\t| ## ASSISTANT (2026-07-20 10:58:23)

[{'type': 'text', 'text': '## TKG 问题的完整背景\n\n### Neuron 的双模型架构\n\nNeuron 硬件（Inferentia/Trainium）的核心约束是：**模型必须预编译为固定形状**。不同于 GPU 可以动态处理任意 batch/seq_len，Neuron 需要在编译时确定输入张量的维度。\n\n因此 NxDI 将一个 LLM 编译成**两个独立的模型**：\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  CTE (Context Encoding Model) — 负责 Prefill        │\n│  - batch_size = 1 (chunked prefill) 或 ctx_batch_size│\n│  - n_active_tokens = max_context_length (大)         │\n│  - 输入: [batch, seq_len] 其中 seq_len 可能是数千    │\n│  - 编译时用 bucketing 支持多种 seq_len              │\n│  - 计算密集：一次处理大量 token                      │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  TKG (Token Generation Model) — 负责 Decode          │\n│  - batch_size = max_num_seqs (如 32)                 │\n│  - n_active_tokens = 1                               │\n│  - 输入: [batch, 1] 每个请求只处理1个新token         │\n│  - 针对 decode 做了专门优化（memory-bound场景）      │\n│  - 吞吐密集：同时处理多个请求的单 token              │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n在**当前的非 chunked prefill 模式**下，调度器严格分离 prefill 和 decode：\n- 有新请求要 prefill → 调用 CTE 模型\n- 所有请求都在 decode → 调用 TKG 模型\n- 两者永远不会同时运行\n\n### Chunked Prefill 改变了什么\n\nChunked prefill 的核心思想是：**把 prefill 和 decode 混在一起处理**。每个 step 里可能同时有：\n- 某个请求的一段 prefill chunk（比如 512 tokens）\n- 其他请求的 decode token（每个 1 token）\n\n所有这些 token 被**拼接成一条长序列**（batch_size=1），一起送入模型。\n\n---\n\n### 两个选项的含义\n\n#### 选项 A: CTE-only（`tkg_model_enabled=false`）\n\n```\n每个 step:\n   所有 token（prefill chunks + decode tokens）\n        ↓ 拼接成 [1, chunk_size]\n        ↓\n   ┌──────────────┐\n   │   CTE 模型    │  ← 唯一的模型\n   └──────────────┘\n        ↓\n   logits [1, chunk_size, vocab_size]\n        ↓\n   按 prefill_completion_state 提取各请求的输出\n```\n\n**特点**：\n- 只编译一个模型，编译时间短\n- 调度简单：所有 step 都走 CTE，不需要判断路由\n- Decode token 也被当作 "chunk_size=1 的 prefill" 处理\n- **劣势**：decode 时效率低。CTE 模型的 n_active_tokens 维度设计为处理大 seq_len，当只有少量 decode token 时（比如 8 个请求各 1 个 token = 总共 8 tokens），输入要 pad 到最小 bucket 大小（如 128），浪费大量计算\n- **适合**：快速验证功能正确性\n\n#### 选项 B: CTE + TKG（`tkg_model_enabled=true`）\n\n```\n每个 step，调度器决定：\n\n情况1: 有 prefill chunk 要处理\n   所有 token（prefill chunks + decode tokens）\n        ↓ 拼接成 [1, chunk_size]\n        ↓\n   ┌──────────────┐\n   │   CTE 模型    │\n   └──────────────┘\n        ↓\n   提取各请求输出\n\n情况2: 所有请求都在 decode（无 prefill chunk）\n   每个请求的最新 token\n        ↓ 形成 [batch_size, 1]\n        ↓\n   ┌──────────────┐\n   │   TKG 模型    │  ← 专门优化的 decode 模型\n   └──────────────┘\n        ↓\n   每个请求的 next token\n```\n\n**特点**：\n- 编译两个模型，编译时间翻倍\n- 调度更复杂：需要判断当前 step 是否有 prefill chunk，决定走 CTE 还是 TKG\n- `is_context_encoding` 的路由逻辑更复杂（之前讨论的那个 `input_ids.shape[-1] > 1` 问题）\n- **优势**：当没有新请求需要 prefill 时（纯 decode step），TKG 模型效率远高于 CTE\n- TKG 的 `[32, 1]` 输入完美匹配 decode 场景，无浪费\n- **适合**：生产环境追求最佳 decode 吞吐\n\n---\n\n### 核心权衡总结\n\n| | CTE-only | CTE + TKG |\n|---|---|---|\n| 编译模型数 | 1 | 2 |\n| 代码复杂度 | 低（无路由逻辑） | 高（需正确判断走哪个模型） |\n| Decode 性能 | 差（pad 浪费） | 好（专用模型） |\n| Prefill 混合性能 | 好 | 好 |\n| Debug 难度 | 低 | 高 |\n| 典型延迟风险 | 纯 decode step 变慢 | 路由错误导致崩溃 |\n\n对于"先跑通再优化"的目标，CTE-only 是默认选择。等功能验证正确后，加上 TKG 是相对独立的增量优化。'}]

[{'type': 'thinking', 'thinking': "The user wants to understand:\n1. How the current code works - is it CTE-only or CTE+TKG?\n2. How does GPU (CUDA) vLLM handle this?\n3. How does Neuron vLLM handle this?\n4. What are the implications of each choice for Neuron vLLM?\n\nLet me think through this systematically based on what I've read from the codebase.\n\n### CUDA vLLM\n\nOn GPU/CUDA, vLLM does NOT have this CTE/TKG split concept at all. There's a single model that handles both prefill and decode:\n- The model is a single PyTorch module that processes any batch size and sequence length dynamically\n- For chunked prefill, the scheduler mixes prefill chunks and decode tokens into one batch, and the model runner processes everything in a single forward pass\n- Flash attention with paged attention handles variable-length sequences efficiently without needing separate compiled models\n\nIn contrast, Neuron vLLM currently uses two separate compiled models: CTE for prefill (batch_size=1, full context length) and TKG for decode (max sequences, seq_len=1), with the scheduler strictly alternating between prefill and decode steps rather than mixing them.\n\nFor chunked prefill, the NxDI codebase has configuration scaffolding that supports both approaches—I'm looking at how `ChunkedPrefillConfig` sets up parameters like max sequences and tile sizes, with a `tkg_model_enabled` flag that defaults to true, suggesting the architecture can handle either keeping TKG enabled during chunked prefill or disabling it entirely.\n\nWhen `tkg_model_enabled=True`, the CTE model handles mixed prefill and decode phases while TKG takes over pure-decode steps; when false, CTE handles everything solo. The CTE gets configured with `batch_size=1` and `n_active_tokens` set to the chunk size, using 2D bucketing across chunk and tile dimensions.\n\nFor the TKG model in chunked prefill mode, after context encoding is enabled, token generation gets configured with `batch_size` matching the maximum number of sequences and `n_active_tokens=1`. Now examining how this affects the Neuron vLLM scheduler and model runner—the native V1 scheduler always produces mixed batches that flow through CTE, and the model runner concatenates all tokens during chunked prefill input preparation.\n\nWhen TKG is enabled, the system needs to make per-step routing decisions between CTE and TKG rather than always using CTE, which opens up optimization opportunities compared to the CTE-only path where decode-only batches still get padded to minimum buckets. all prefills are done. ## ASSISTANT (2026-07-20 11:09:53)

[{'type': 'text', 'text': '## CUDA vLLM 的做法\n\nGPU 上**根本不存在 CTE/TKG 的概念**。原因是 GPU 支持动态形状：\n\n```\nCUDA vLLM: 单一模型，任意形状\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  同一个 LlamaForCausalLM 实例               │\n│                                             │\n│  Step 1: prefill [1, 4096] → Flash Attn    │\n│  Step 2: decode  [32, 1]   → Flash Attn    │\n│  Step 3: mixed   [1, 2048+32个decode token] │ ← chunked prefill\n│                                             │\n│  全部走同一个 model.forward()               │\n│  Flash Attention / PagedAttention 天然支持  │\n│  异构序列长度                                │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\nGPU 的 chunked prefill 非常自然：\n- 一个模型，一次 forward 同时处理 prefill chunks + decode tokens\n- Paged attention kernel 通过 `block_table` + `slot_mapping` 处理不同长度的 KV cache\n- 无需任何路由逻辑，无需编译两个模型\n\n---\n\n## Neuron vLLM 当前（非 chunked prefill）\n\n当前 Neuron 是 **CTE + TKG 双模型，严格分离**：\n\n```\n当前 Neuron vLLM 架构:\n\nContinuousBatchingNeuronScheduler\n    │\n    ├── 有新请求要 prefill？\n    │       ↓ YES\n    │   隐藏所有 decode 请求（holdback）\n    │   只调度 1 个 prefill 请求\n    │       ↓\n    │   ┌─────────────────────────────┐\n    │   │ CTE 模型                     │\n    │   │ shape: [1, seq_len]          │\n    │   │ seq_len pad 到 bucket 边界   │\n    │   │ KV: contiguous 布局          │\n    │   │ (每个 seq 一整块连续内存)     │\n    │   └─────────────────────────────┘\n    │\n    └── 没有新请求 prefill？\n            ↓ 所有请求都在 decode\n        ┌─────────────────────────────┐\n        │ TKG 模型                     │\n        │ shape: [batch_size, 1]       │\n        │ batch pad 到 max_num_seqs    │\n        │ KV: 同一块 contiguous 内存   │\n        │ (通过 seq_id 访问各自行)     │\n        └─────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n关键点：\n- **严格串行**：prefill 和 decode 永远不会在同一个 step 里发生\n- **prefill 阻塞 decode**：长 prefill 期间所有 decode 请求等待 → 高 TPOT\n- CTE 和 TKG **共享同一块 KV cache 内存**（contiguous layout，通过 `seq_id` 索引到各自的"行"）\n- `max_prompt_batch_size = 1`：每次只 prefill 一个请求\n\n---\n\n## Neuron vLLM 加入 Chunked Prefill 后的两种选择\n\n### 选项 A: CTE-only（`tkg_model_enabled=false`）\n\n```\nvLLM V1 Native Scheduler (chunked prefill enabled)\n    │\n    │ 每个 step 输出 mixed batch:\n    │   req_A: prefill chunk [512 tokens]\n    │   req_B: decode [1 token]\n    │   req_C: decode [1 token]\n    │\n    ↓ 全部拼接成 [1, 514]\n┌──────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│ CTE 模型 (唯一模型)                       │\n│                                          │\n│ 编译形状: [1, bucket_chunk_size]          │\n│ buckets: [[128,tiles],[256,tiles],...]    │\n│ 514 tokens → pad 到 bucket 边界 (如 640) │\n│                                          │\n│ KV cache: block 布局 (paged attention)   │\n│ slot_mapping 指定每个 token 写哪个 block │\n│ block_table 指定每个 seq 的 block 列表   │\n└──────────────────────────────────────────┘\n    │\n    ↓ logits [1, 514, vocab_size] (去 pad 后)\n    ↓ 按 prefill_completion_state 提取:\n        req_A: prefill 未完成 → mask to -inf\n        req_B: decode → 取第 513 位的 logits → sample\n        req_C: decode → 取第 514 位的 logits → sample\n```\n\n**对 Neuron 系统的影响**：\n\n| 方面 | 影响 |\n|------|------|\n| 编译 | 只编译 1 个 NEFF，编译时间 ~1x |\n| 调度 | 简单 — 每个 step 都走 CTE，无路由判断 |\n| KV cache | 必须用 block 布局（不再是 contiguous） |\n| 纯 decode step | **效率差** — 比如 8 个 decode token 拼接后只有 8 tokens，pad 到最小 bucket（128），93% 算力浪费 |\n| 内存 | 只需一个模型的权重 |\n| 正确性风险 | 低 — 只有一条代码路径 |\n\n### 选项 B: CTE + TKG（`tkg_model_enabled=true`）\n\n```\nvLLM V1 Native Scheduler\n    │\n    │ 判断当前 step 类型:\n    │\n    ├─── 有 prefill chunk？\n    │       ↓ YES: 走 CTE\n    │   所有 token 拼接成 [1, chunk_size]\n    │   ┌──────────────────────────────┐\n    │   │ CTE 模型                      │\n    │   │ [1, padded_chunk_size]        │\n    │   │ block KV cache                │\n    │   │ 处理 prefill + decode tokens  │\n    │   └──────────────────────────────┘\n    │\n    └─── 全部是 decode？\n            ↓ YES: 走 TKG\n        ┌──────────────────────────────┐\n        │ TKG 模型                      │\n        │ [batch_size, 1]               │\n        │ block KV cache (同一块)       │\n        │ 专为 decode 优化              │\n        └──────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n**对 Neuron 系统的影响**：\n\n| 方面 | 影响 |\n|------|------|\n| 编译 | 编译 2 个 NEFF，编译时间 ~2x |\n| 调度 | 复杂 — 需要判断 "本 step 是否有 prefill chunk" 来路由 |\n| KV cache | 两个模型共享同一块 block KV cache，读写必须一致 |\n| 纯 decode step | **效率好** — TKG 的 [32, 1] 完美匹配，零浪费 |\n| 内存 | 两份模型权重（但 KV cache 共享） |\n| 正确性风险 | 高 — 路由判断、KV 一致性、切换时序都可能出错 |\n\n---\n\n## 路由判断的核心难题（CTE+TKG 模式特有）\n\n现有 NxDI 的 `is_context_encoding` 判断：\n\n```python\n# model_base.py:3348\nis_context_encoding = input_ids.shape[-1] > 1 and not position_ids.min().item()\n```\n\n这在 chunked prefill 下**会出错**：\n\n| 场景 | input_ids.shape[-1] | position_ids.min() | 判断结果 | 正确行为 |\n|------|-----|-----|------|------|\n| 纯 prefill chunk（新请求） | >1 | 0 | CTE ✓ | CTE |\n| prefill chunk 续传（从 pos 512 开始） | >1 | 512 | **TKG ✗** | 应走 CTE |\n| prefill + decode 混合 | >1 | 可能是 0 也可能不是 | 不确定 | 应走 CTE |\n| 纯 decode | >1（因为拼接了多个请求的 decode token） | >0 | **TKG** | 应走 TKG |\n\n如果选 CTE-only，这个判断完全不需要——永远走 CTE。\n如果选 CTE+TKG，需要在 model runner 层面告诉模型"这个 step 有没有 prefill chunk"，不能靠 tensor 形状推断。\n\n---\n\n## 总结：对 Neuron vLLM 的实际工程影响\n\n| | CTE-only | CTE + TKG |\n|---|---|---|\n| 需要改的 NxDI 代码 | 少（移除 NotImplementedError，加 chunked dispatch，改 logit 提取） | 多（上述 + 路由逻辑 + TKG 也需要支持 block KV） |\n| Model Runner 改动 | 几乎不需要（已有 `_prepare_chunked_prefill_inputs`） | 需要加 "判断是否有 prefill chunk → 切换模型" 的逻辑 |\n| 当前 TKG 是否现成可用 | N/A | 现有 TKG 在 contiguous KV 布局下工作；block KV 下的 TKG 需要验证 `_get_cache_for_chunked_prefill` 在 TKG 路径是否正确 |\n| Decode 吞吐退化 | 有（pad 浪费 50-90%） | 无 |\n| 首次验证时间 | 快 | 慢（要确保两个模型 KV 互通） |\n\n**建议**：CTE-only 先跑通验证正确性，确认 block KV + chunked attention kernel 工作正常后，再加 TKG 作为性能优化。TKG 是纯增量改动，不影响已有功能。'}]
